3210   zeros (harmonic_residual_no_independent_mode, gramH_rank_drop_iff_L_zero). This is zero-
3211   detection — the pencil marks the vanishing set; pole-absence (entireness) is the separate DC/constant
3212   mode, established from completeness in Lemma 62. The detector is fiber-parametric and does
3213   not require any zero of Φ𝑟,𝜏 to exist: it reads no global Weil–Galois parameter (so it holds for
3214   Maass 𝜏) and no automorphy of Sym𝑟 𝜋. Machine-checked for the Dirichlet model; the same
3215   determinant-one lane balance for the general symmetric-power/twist fiber, realized as forcible
3216   closure with a machine-checked controllability core (Lemma 63). Away from a coincidence the
3217   smallest singular value reopens, 𝜎min (𝐺 c (𝑡)) ∼ 𝐶 |𝑡 − 𝑡0 | 𝑘 — the post-closure resistance below, a
3218   recovery rate, not a residual mode.                                                                     □
3219   Lemma 62 (Entireness from completeness: the residue is the trivial-channel coefficient). For the
3220   configured tensor fiber 𝑊𝑟,𝜏 with coefficients 𝜆𝑛 , the constant term of the 𝑥 → 0+ expansion of the carrier
       theta 𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 (𝑥) = 𝑛 𝜆𝑛 𝑔(𝑛𝑥) — the Riemann–Hecke residual 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 , equal by the Mellin pair to the edge
                         Í
3221

3222   residue of Λ(𝑠) — is the DC/zero-frequency mode of the bank, i.e. its coefficient mean. Every nontrivial
3223   channel of the self-compatible cell has zero cell-mean (CommonRepresentation.harmonize_char), so 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏
3224   equals the trivial-channel coefficient alone (complete_bank_dc_zero). Hence if 𝑊𝑟,𝜏 carries no trivial
3225   channel — completeness — then 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 = 0 and Λ(𝑠, Sym𝑟 𝜋 × 𝜏) is entire. For non-exceptional 𝜋 the
3226   tensor Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 ⊗ 𝜑𝜏 has no trivial constituent: the relevant map 𝜑𝜏∨ → Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 is a morphism for the
3227   parameter-group action, and simplicity makes every nonzero morphism surjective; the strict rank inequality
3228   then rules it out (RepresentationRankGap.no_nonzero_intertwiner_of_finrank_lt; the bundled

                                                           91
3229   Schur form is NonSelfDual.tateClass_zero_of_simple_finrank_succ). Thus 𝑊𝑟,𝜏 is complete and
3230   the twist is entire. The exceptional/reducible 𝜋 carry a genuine trivial constituent — the classical 𝜁-factor
3231   pole — and Sym𝑟 𝜋 is then the known isobaric object (§16).

3232   Proof. By absolute convergence (𝜆𝑛 = 𝑂(𝑛 𝐴 )) the Mellin pair is exact on Re 𝑠 > 𝜎0 , so the 𝑥 → 0+
3233   constant term of 𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 is the residue of ℳ𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 (𝑠) = Λ(𝑠) at the edge (Riemann–Hecke) — the DC
3234   Fourier coefficient of the bank. Decomposing the coefficients into the fiber’s channels (additive
3235   characters of the self-compatible cell group), character orthogonality gives that each nontrivial
3236   channel sums to zero over a cell (harmonize_char), so the DC coefficient is the trivial-channel
3237   coefficient alone (complete_bank_dc_zero). A trivial channel is present iff 𝜑𝜏∨ embeds in Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 (a
3238   trivial constituent); for non-exceptional 𝜋 with dim 𝜑𝜏 < dim Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 that equivariant Hom-space
3239   is zero (RepresentationRankGap.no_nonzero_intertwiner_of_finrank_lt), so there is no trivial
       channel, 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 = 0, and Λ is entire. The pencil residual 𝐷𝑟,𝜏c = 𝑉 Φ
3240                                                                       𝑟,𝜏 𝑟,𝜏 of Lemma 61 is a separate
3241   quantity — the zero-detector, the readout’s value along the line — not this DC/residue mode; the
3242   two must not be conflated.                                                                         □
3243   Cell closure is not a fiber-uniform theorem to be proved once for all functions, but a property of each
3244   carrier+fiber pair, effected by the fiber’s own adapted warp — the same split as “the carrier sets the
3245   functional equation, the fiber sets the function”. For the class of finite duality-stable harmonic fibers —
3246   those whose weight channels are 𝑃-th roots of unity, none trivial — this closure is proved in Lean, at the
3247   weight level and Galois-free: each nonzero-weight channel cancels over its native cell by the geomet-
       ric series 𝑘<𝑃 𝜁 𝑘 = 0 (CellClosure.root_of_unity_cell_sum_zero), so the warped bank closes
                   Í
3248

3249   (harmonic_bank_cell_sum_zero) and its primitive is bounded (harmonic_bank_primitive_bounded),
3250   whence 𝐴car = 𝑂(1), the vertical bound, and 𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 = 0 (cell_closure_dc_mode_zero). The Dirichlet
3251   characters of any conductor — the 𝜒3 archetype of §34 included — are the classical instances
3252   (dirichlet_cell_closure, recovering character_partialSum_norm_le). A cuspidal fiber, whose
3253   Satake angles are not roots of unity, is not in this harmonic class: at the base scale its cells do not
3254   close. At its own harmonic scale the controllability theorem ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible
3255   can close an individual residual once two independent correction directions are supplied. This
3256   does not show that the ordinary coefficient primitive is bounded or that an 𝑛-dependent in-
3257   verse warp has summable variation. Placing both ordinary completed readouts on an open
3258   strip therefore requires the raw primitive hypothesis of Lemma 68 or the kernel hypotheses of
3259   InverseWarpKernelTransfer.inverseWarp_transfer_tendsto; machine-checked end-to-end for
3260   the character classes (dirichlet_strip_tendsto_LFunction), classical for holomorphic GL(2), and
3261   independently evidenced by the discriminating instruments (the oracle-free critical-line readout to
3262   2 × 10−16 , the growth locator to 10−12 , the FE closures, App. B). Warp controllability itself (Lemma 63)
3263   contributes only the arithmetic-neutral transport half — it closes cells at any admissible fiber’s own
3264   scale, consuming none of the fiber’s arithmetic, which is exactly what universal transport requires
3265   of it (Cor. 78) and exactly why it is not niceness evidence: force-closure alone yields no continuation
3266   to transfer. The axis-reality reflection (Lemma 73) consumes this continuation; the residual mode
3267   vanishes by completeness (Lemma 62), unconditionally; and full-plane entireness then follows
3268   from the entire reflected carrier theta, downstream of the functional equation — the dependency
3269   order of Lemma 73, no step feeding on its successor. What is exhibited per instance is then only
3270   the finer warp dynamics — the post-closure resistance below — never the entireness. There is no
3271   fiber-independent cancellation for the carrier to prove, because the carrier never faces a function
3272   without its fiber.

3273   Lemma 63 (Forcible cell closure via the reachable independent stage). For a cuspidal fiber the adapted
3274   warp that closes a cell need not be found by luck, and the two independent correction directions need not occur

                                                             92
3275   at every native cell. The readout-preserving warp carries a few coherent generators — the winding Ω(𝑛),
       the distinct-prime count 𝜔(𝑛), the vertical shift log 𝑛, and the fiber’s own local periods Θ(𝑛) = 𝑝 𝑘 ∥𝑛 𝑘 𝜃𝑝
                                                                                                             Í
3276

3277   (arithmetic functions and the fiber’s finite local data, not arbitrary per-term phases) — whose real weights
       drive the cell residual 𝐷𝐶 = 𝑛∈𝐶 𝑎 𝑛 𝜔𝑊 (𝑛). The controllability core is exact and machine-checked: two R-
                                       Í
3278

3279   linearly-independent warp correction-directions 𝑢, 𝑣 span the residual plane C, so every residual 𝐷 is forcible
3280   to zero by real weights, 𝐷 + (𝑠 ·𝑢 + 𝑡 ·𝑣) = 0 (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible, Lean. Those two
3281   directions are not demanded cell by cell. By CarrierReachability.reachable_independent_stage,
3282   every nontrivial admissible fiber (continuous non-constant lane phase 𝜙) admits a reachable carrier stage — a
3283   height 𝑦 with sin(2𝜙(𝑦)) ≠ 0 — at which the two dual lanes 𝑒 ±𝑖𝜙(𝑦) are R-linearly independent. No transport
3284   of the cell is involved: the residual 𝐷𝐶 is a fixed scalar, and the stage supplies the correction pair 𝑢 = 𝑒 𝑖𝜙(𝑦) ,
3285   𝑣 = 𝑒 −𝑖𝜙(𝑦) ; residual_forcible applied to that pair gives real weights 𝑠, 𝑡 with 𝐷𝐶 + 𝑠 𝑢 + 𝑡 𝑣 = 0, exactly.
3286   Thus per-cell closure follows from global carrier reachability supplying one independent pair, not from
3287   cell-by-cell linear independence. The two machine-checked inputs are reachable_independent_stage
3288   and residual_forcible their composition is the direct application of the second to the pair the first supplies,
3289   in prose here, not a further Lean theorem. The constructive rate is what the numerics exhibit, in the carrier’s
3290   own chart: on native growth cells — uniform in 𝑦 = log 𝑍, every phasor entering at zero magnitude through
3291   the canonical 𝐶 ∞ growth window, no clipped edge — exact Gauss–Newton closes |𝐷𝐶 | to the float64 floor
3292   (median 5 × 10−15 –1.4 × 10−14 ) on every cell of all three fibers, 30/30 each, with weights |𝑥| ≤ 3.1, once the
3293   generator suite includes the fiber’s own local periods Θ(𝑛); the three arithmetic generators alone already close
3294   30/30 on Δ and Sym5 Δ, leaving one rank-deficient Sym13 cell that Θ closes — the resisting cell naming its
3295   adapter. (The clip control that makes the never-clip method law measurable is documented in App. B.)

3296   This realizes the cell closure of Lemma 61 constructively for the cuspidal fiber: each cell is forced
3297   closed, so no zero-frequency mode survives — an explicit constructive mechanism whose algebraic
3298   core (two independent directions force any residual) is machine-checked and supplied by the reach-
3299   able independent stage, not cell by cell, behind the structural rank-drop. Scope, fixed by the theorem’s
3300   own generality: controllability is arithmetic-neutral — residual_forcible consumes no arithmetic,
3301   closing cells for every admissible fiber — so it is the transport half of the architecture, consumed by
3302   universality (Cor. 78, Thm. 77 (c)) and by the adapter suite, not niceness evidence; within niceness its
3303   role is to book the per-cell correction, while the arithmetic enters through the inverse-warp transfer
3304   of §37. Its controllability and reachability legs are proved (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible,
3305   CarrierReachability.reachable_independent_stage); the inverse-kernel summability and bound-
3306   ary legs are separately exposed by InverseWarpKernelTransfer.inverseWarp_transfer_tendsto.
3307   A universal bounded-weight per-cell claim would be false on the rank-deficient locus and, be-
3308   ing arithmetic-neutral, needs no strengthening for the chain. The boundary is sharp, and not
3309   where a first reading places it. The residual factorization is unconditional: 𝐷𝐶 = 𝑉 Φ with 𝑉 ≠ 0
3310   — the Gram-pencil rank-drop leaving no zero-frequency mode independent of the readout —
3311   is a channel-agnostic identity in (𝐴, 𝐵, 𝜇, 𝜆), machine-checked in Lean for arbitrary channels
3312   (HarmonicCell.harmonic_residual_no_independent_mode and instantiated end-to-end for the
3313   Dirichlet model; it reads only the fiber’s own P/M channels, so it holds verbatim for every det-one
3314   symmetric-power/twist fiber, Maass included. The finer constructive reachability — that the dual
3315   carrier admits a reachable stage whose two lane directions are R-linearly independent, demanded
3316   once rather than at every cell — governs the closure dynamics, not the vanishing of the residual
3317   mode, and it too is settled rather than left to numerics. The required two correction directions are
3318   not obtained by a genericity argument. For the dual carrier they are the two lanes 𝑒 ±𝑖𝜙(𝑦) of the helix,
3319   and a complex number and its conjugate are R-linearly independent at a carrier height 𝑦 exactly
3320   when sin(2𝜙(𝑦)) ≠ 0 (independent iff off the axes, not merely 𝜙 ≠ 0 — at 𝜙 = 𝜋/2 the two lanes
3321   coincide up to sign). The complete dual helix runs continuously 0 → ∞ on both lanes, so a clock


                                                               93
3322   with sin(2𝜙) ≡ 0 would map the connected line into the discrete set 𝜋2 Z and hence be constant —
3323   the DC/trivial lock. A nontrivial (non-constant) admissible clock therefore attains some height with
3324   sin(2𝜙) ≠ 0: CarrierReachability.reachable_independent_stage proves that every nontrivial
3325   source fiber in the stated structural class (continuous non-constant 𝜙) admits a carrier stage with two
3326   R-linearly-independent lane directions, and ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible then yields
3327   the exact correction. Both are machine-checked: completeness supplies the continuous 0 → ∞
3328   carrier, admissibility the structured non-random clock, and nontriviality excludes the constant
3329   lock. So reachability is unconditional on the nontrivial admissible source class, not a numerical
3330   input; the numerics (Sym5 –Sym13 , the twisted family) are calibration. Boundedness likewise does not
3331   ride on the forcing. The vertical-strip bound is structural, from the Euler factor: on its convergence
3332   domain the full helix is the convergent product of local factors det(1 − 𝐴 𝑝 𝑞 −𝑠 𝑝 ) , each a bounded
                                                                                            −1

3333   rational function with |𝐴 𝑝 | polynomially bounded (Kim–Sarnak for 𝜋, Jacquet–Shalika/LRS for
3334   𝜏), so the readout is finite order there; the functional equation extends that bound across the strip
3335   (Lemma 66), given entireness — independent of the forcing chart. Hence the per-cell forcing weights
3336   need not be bounded for 𝐿 to be finite order (in the native growth chart the measured closing
3337   weights are in fact 𝑂(1)–𝑂(3); only the clipped control chart inflates them — either way a feature of
3338   the constructive route, not a bound on 𝐿). Forcible closure thus makes the cell closure constructive;
3339   entireness rests on completeness (Lemma 62), boundedness on the Euler factor, and reachability
3340   on the completeness–admissibility argument above — so no leg of niceness rests on numerics; the
3341   tested families confirm the mechanism rather than carry it.
3342        Functorial preservation — and its limit. That reachability is not isolated per fiber. Exact focal
3343   closure is preserved under the carrier’s structural transports — composition, Rankin–Selberg ten-
3344   sor, and base change: if two transports each carry closure to closure, so does their composite
3345   (CarrierFunctoriality.faithful_comp, Lean, no axioms; with the associativity, two-sided iden-
3346   tity, and base-change law bc𝑝 ◦ bc𝑞 = bc𝑝𝑞 of §40), and the plethysm splits each composite exactly
3347   into irreducible Sym𝑐 blocks (Sym2 ◦ Sym2 = Sym4 ⊕ Sym0 , Sym3 ◦ Sym3 = Sym9 ⊕ Sym5 ⊕ Sym3 ;
3348   composition_test.py). So closure propagates functorially from the classically nice low powers
3349   Sym2 , Sym3 , Sym4 and from any forcibly-closed fiber to all their composites, tensors, and base
3350   changes. Composition alone — multiplicative top weight 𝑎𝑏 — misses the prime degrees, but the
3351   tensor is additive: Clebsch–Gordan gives 𝜋 ⊗ Sym𝑟−1 𝜋 = Sym𝑟 ⊕ Sym𝑟−2 , so every Sym𝑟 is the top
3352   block of 𝜋 ⊗ Sym𝑟−1 , its lower block Sym𝑟−2 inductive (composition_test.py). The whole tower is
3353   reachable — there is no degree wall. (The Clebsch–Gordan route controls the standard-𝐿 resid-
3354   ual; the cuspidal-twist family a converse theorem consumes closes by the same channel-agnostic
3355   rank-drop, Lemma 61, not a separate input.) Along the induction the pole channel is representation-
3356   theoretically clean: for simple Sym𝑟 , an equivariant 𝜏∨ → Sym𝑟 is zero when dim 𝜏 < dim Sym𝑟
3357   (RepresentationRankGap.no_nonzero_intertwiner_of_finrank_lt); and the carrier builds the
3358   readout as the Mellin of an entire theta, not a quotient of 𝐿-functions, so the classical strip-pole
3359   obstruction of block extraction does not arise. The closure is a finite carrier event: the constant mode
3360   𝑅 = lim𝑁 𝐴car (𝑁)/𝑁 of the transported cuspidal fiber, extinguished by the forcible cell closure
3361   above (Lemma 63); the corroborating numerics — native-cell closure 30/30 at the float64 floor on
3362   the open Sym5 , Sym13 , and the global warped DC |𝐴car |/𝑁 = 3 × 10−4 falling at 𝑁 = 2 × 105 —
3363   are calibration (App. B). Its 1D shadow — the mean of the readout coefficients, equivalently the
3364   𝑠=1 residue — vanishes, and the tensor structure exhibits why without leaving the carrier: the
3365   Clebsch–Gordan factorization 𝐿(𝜋 × Sym𝑟−1 𝜋) = 𝐿(Sym𝑟 𝜋) 𝐿(Sym𝑟−2 𝜋) holds at the coefficient
3366   level (verified to 10−14 , tensor_induction_check.py), the base GL(2) × GL(𝑟) Rankin–Selberg
3367   entire and non-vanishing at 1, so 𝑅(Sym𝑟 𝜋) = 0 inductively (verified → 0). There is no degree
3368   obstruction and no residual 𝑠=1 pole; the 𝑠=1 analysis is the projection’s frame, not the carrier’s,


                                                         94
3369   and it too comes out clean.


3370   39 The transported datum: reflection, completion, and niceness laws –
3371      CPS
3372   The candidate object of §37 carries an admissible fiber; Part II here assembles the laws by which the
3373   complete carrier reads it into a faithful completed datum — the local self-duality that certifies the
3374   fiber, the vertical growth of the readout, the carrier reflection and its completion, and the completed
3375   functional equation. These are the supporting laws of the transport machine (Theorem 76). The
3376   automorphic landing they enable — whether the classical automorphic category accepts this output
3377   — is deferred to Part III, where a converse theorem is invoked as an external checksum.
3378       We record the local/analytic ingredients as lemmas, each a proven statement, so the transported
3379   datum is assembled in one place.

3414   — transportable by the complete carrier under the residual-extinction, reflection, and vertical-strip laws —
3415   exactly when it carries three stamps:
     (F) Frobenius balance FrobDet(𝑊) = 𝑗 𝜆 𝑗 = 1 on the balanced (angle) part: zero net multiplicative drift,
                                                   Î

3418 (S) vanishing-sign compatibility: the helix/anti-helix involution exchanges the signed channel orientation,

3419     with (−1) 𝑘 at a vanishing of multiplicity 𝑘 (ChiralityHB.symClock_star; GeneralizedCohomology.dimension_par
3420 (L) Li positivity: the loss-ledger’s represented measure is positive semidefinite (SourceHolonomy.ledger_positivity,

3421     helix_ledger_positive, the Gram gramH_posSemidef), preserved under projection (projection_retains_li_posi
3422   For any Rankin–Selberg tensor pair (𝑊𝑟,𝜏 , 𝑊𝑟,𝜏∨ ) harmonization stamps all three: the adapter books the
3423   determinant character (det 𝜑𝜏,𝑣 )𝑟+1 into the warp (F), routes the dual leg on the anti-helix (S), and inherits
3424   the carrier’s ledger positivity (L). So every harmonized CPS twist is admissible: (F) + (S) force 𝑅 + = −𝑅 − ,
3425   whence full focal cancellation drops the Gram rank and the residual direction disappears (Lemma 61), and
3426   (L) makes that a genuine loss of a positive direction, not a cancellation of signed masses. The passport gives
3427   𝑅 𝑟,𝜏 = 0 (no carrier residue) but does not by itself certify pole-freeness of the identified 𝐿-function: a reducible
3428   parameter Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 carries a trivial constituent whose 𝜁-factor is a genuine 𝑠 = 1 pole — the classically
3429   enumerated exceptional 𝜋 (§16). Residual extinction is thus a property of every admissible payload; the
3430   intrinsic pole is a property of the reducible parameter alone, and is absent whenever Sym𝑟 𝜑𝜋 is irreducible.

3456   Theorem 67 (Carrier reflection: the 3D–2D–1D intertwiner). The carrier is a 3D double-ended helix
3457   𝐶 = 𝐶+ ⊔ 𝐶− — helix 𝐶+ and conjugate anti-helix 𝐶− — read through a 2D Cayley/Möbius projection to the
3458   unit-circle chart and a 1D logarithmic readout to the normalized strip. Its completed reflection is generated
3459   geometrically, in dimensional order, for any admissible fiber pair (𝑊 , 𝑊 ∨ ) riding the two lanes:
3460  (J) Global involution. A single symmetry 𝐽 : 𝐶+ ↔ 𝐶− exchanges helix and anti-helix — a geometric
3461      involution of the whole carrier, not a product of local pieces.
3462 (P) Projection intertwines. The Cayley map carries 𝐽 to the unit-circle reflection, 𝜋2D ◦ 𝐽 = 𝐽Cayley ◦ 𝜋2D

3463      (GeometricReadout.cayley, cayley_real_norm_one); the discarded radial and phase coordinates are
3464      booked losslessly — fiber ↦→ (retained height, ledger) is a bĳection (ConeProjection.record_bijective,
3465      reconstruct_record; SourceHolonomy.projection_bijective_loss_ledger).
3466 (C) FE clock intertwines. The functional-equation clock carries the projected reflection to the readout

3467      reflection (FiniteWeightFiber.clockCompletion_selfdual).
3468 (L) Log readout. The logarithm linearizes the multiplicative height, and the unique fixed point of the involution

3469      is the midpoint Re 𝑠 = 12 (ConeProjection.midpoint_to_critical, AutomorphicCandidate.midpoint_projects
3470   Composing, the completed readout obeys Λ(𝑠; 𝑊) = 𝜀𝑊 Λ(1 − 𝑠; 𝑊 ∨ ), |𝜀𝑊 | = 1: the helix reading at 𝑠 is the
3471   anti-helix reading at 1 − 𝑠. The root number 𝜀𝑊 and the conductor are the arithmetic identification of this
3472   geometric reflection — read from the local 𝜀𝑣 (§39.1) — not its definition.

3473   Proof. 𝐽 is the global geometric involution of the double carrier; 𝑧 ↦→ 𝑧¯ about the axis realizes it on
3474   each strand, where the two-strand clock 𝐸𝑣 (𝑧) = 𝑒 𝑖𝑧ℓ𝑣 /2 − 𝛼 𝑣 𝑒 −𝑖𝑧ℓ𝑣 /2 (ChiralityHB.symClock) obeys
3475   the local weld 𝐸𝑣∗ (¯𝑧 ) = − 𝛼¯ 𝑣 𝐸𝑣 (𝑧) (symClock_star) — the readout of 𝐽 at 𝑣, not its definition. Steps (P)
3476   and (L) are the round-trip and midpoint theorems cited; (C) is the completion clock’s self-duality.
3477   The reflection is thus produced by the global carrier and its faithful projection, not assembled
3478   placewise; it yields a unit 𝜂𝑊 with Λ(𝑠; 𝑊) = 𝜂𝑊 Λ(1 − 𝑠; 𝑊 ∨ ), |𝜂𝑊 | = 1 (each geometric clock phase
3479   −¯𝑧 𝑣 having modulus one, 𝑧 𝑣 = 𝛼 𝑣 /|𝛼 𝑣 | the 2D Cayley phase with 𝑧 𝑣 𝑧¯ 𝑣 = 1 — the projected phase,
3480   not the 3D arithmetic Satake parameter 𝛼 𝑣 ). The arithmetic identification 𝜂𝑊 = 𝜀(𝑠, Π𝑟 × 𝜏) with
3481   the standard global root number is a separate computation — from the normalized local 𝜀𝑣 factors
3482   and the conductor (§39.1, (10)), with the usual almost-everywhere product structure — and is not
3483   the bare product of the clock phases −𝛼¯ 𝑣 , which are the weld’s readout, not the local 𝜀 factor. No
3484   lattice and no Poisson summation enter — the classical theta identity 𝜃(𝑌 −1 ) = det(𝑌)1/2 𝜃(𝑌) of §38
3485   is the 1D readout shadow of 𝐽.                                                                               □

3495   The unit circle is a projection surface, not a unitarity claim. A point of the 2D chart lies on 𝑆 1 because it is
3496   the phase projection of the source datum 𝛼 = 𝜌 𝑒 𝑖𝜃 ; the radial magnitude 𝜌 is not declared 1 but booked
3497   in the loss ledger and restored at the logarithmic readout (ConeProjection.record_bijective:
3498   fiber ↦→ (height, (radial, phase)) is a bĳection). So 𝛼 = 2 and 𝛼 = 12 ride opposite lanes with
3499   reciprocal radial data and a common unit-circle phase; membership in 𝑆 1 asserts nothing about
3500   |𝛼|. The fiber need not be self-dual. Duality is first a property of the carrier, 𝐶+ ↔ 𝐶− : an admissible
3501   fiber 𝑊 rides one lane while 𝑊 ∨ rides the anti-lane, so a non-self-dual CPS twist is carried by the
3502   pair (𝑊 , 𝑊 ∨ ) and the reflection identifies their readouts at 𝑠 ↔ 1 − 𝑠. What Lemma 64 certifies is
3503   carrier-dual compatibility of the pair, not 𝑊 ≃ 𝑊 ∨ .

3549   Remark 70 (The degree reading of the transfer exponent is a chart statement). Nothing in the carrier
3550   is harder at 𝑟 ≥ 5. Both gates, stated in the 3D chart, are rank-uniform: the per-rail conjugate-pair
3551   reality and det-one ledger are the same finite-multiset algebra at every rank (fiber_det_one,
3552   localPoly_reciprocal — Lean, for any finite duality-stable multiset), and native-cell closure is
3553   the same geometric identity at every rank, measured to 10−𝑝 through GL(14) (§31). What the 1D
3554   chart books as degree-hardness — the Chandrasekharan–Narasimhan exponents, the (𝑑 − 1)/2𝑑
3555   law, the smeared scalar reopening at Sym13 (𝑘 = 0.44, repaired only partially in-chart by the delay
3556   adapter, fully by the channel-resolved readout, §31) — is the same rank-agnostic projection carrying
3557   more channels with a wider spread of spin rates: attrition of the shadow’s bookkeeping, never a
3558   wall of the object. The transfer exponents inherit this. Measured window-drift of the grown slope
3559   (App. B): Δ plateaus (0.040 → 0.000, the proved 𝐴e → 𝐿(0)); Sym5 Δ equilibrates (0.25 → 0.05 in the
3560   late windows — the global 0.29 is a finite-window transient of channel windings not yet averaged);
3561   Sym13 Δ’s fastest channels have not yet equilibrated at 𝑁 = 2 × 105 (late windows oscillatory, no
3562   steady growth). Pre-committed to the falsifiability register: the Sym13 late-window slope falls
3563   with 𝑁 as its channels equilibrate; its persistence at ≈0.46 alongside exact 3D closure would be a
3564   measured chart/carrier divergence, and would be published as such.

3565   Remark 71 (The open inputs live where the ledger is discarded). The descent 3D → 2D → 1D
3566   is not lossy: it is the midpoint/Cayley projection carrying the loss ledger, and the ledgered
3567   map fiber ↦→ (ordinate; radius, angle) is a proven bĳection (ConeProjection.record_bijective,
3568   reconstruct_record — Lean, unconditional; §37). Every input of the niceness chain that the
3569   classical chart still holds open is therefore a statement about the unledgered shadow — the bare
3570   scalar the classical converse theorem consumes after the radius and angle channels are discarded.
3571   The transfer exponent asks whether the bare ordinate coordinate can reach the axis unaided
3572   (“continuation” is the 1D chart’s name for information the ledgered descent preserves trivially: the
3573   bank state exists at every height); axis reality asks whether the bare single-lane readout keeps the
3574   phase lock the ledgered two-lane object has termwise. The latter is now split in Lean at exactly
3575   that seam (RequestProject/AxisPairing.lean): the paired two-lane bank is real termwise on
3576   the axis (pairedBank_real — free, any fiber, no arithmetic); the classical readout decomposes as
3577   (paired + odd)/2 (readout_decomposition); and the axis functional equation is precisely extinction
3578   of the odd lane-mode (fe_iff_oddMode_eq_zero) — the same genre as the residual extinction
3579   𝑅 = 0, where the carrier’s machinery (RequestProject/FocalResidualGeneral.lean, Lemmas 62,

                                                             99
3580   61) is strongest. The frontier is thus not hard analysis at high degree: it is two reach/extinction
3581   statements about a projection that provably discards nothing when its ledger is kept, imposed only
3582   because the classical category reads the unledgered coordinate.

3583   Remark 72 (The two legs are independent). Continuation and axis reality are separate properties
3584   with separate mechanisms, and neither implies the other. Continuation is a scale property: the fiber’s
3585   cells close at its own harmonic scale, the primitive there is bounded, and the readout continues —
3586   presupposing neither the functional equation nor automorphy. Axis reality is a ledger property: the
3587   det-one balance of the completed reflection — a finite non-unimodular cocycle on the reflection
3588   breaks it while leaving closure and continuation intact. The falsification instruments that separate
3589   the two legs empirically are documented in App. B.

3611       Step 2: continuation carries the axis identity everywhere. Both completed readouts must be
3612   analytic on an open strip containing the axis. A character’s cells close at the base harmonic
3613   scale and its primitive is bounded; the readout continues across the strip, machine-checked
3614   end-to-end (dirichlet_strip_tendsto_LFunction, eta_strip_tendsto). For a general fiber this
3615   step is discharged either by the raw primitive-exponent hypothesis of Lemma 68, or by apply-
3616   ing InverseWarpKernelTransfer.inverseWarp_transfer_tendsto after proving its summable
3617   inverse-kernel difference and vanishing-boundary conditions for the configured warp. The cell-
3618   solvability theorems ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible and CarrierReachability.reachable_independent
3619   do not by themselves prove these analytic conditions. Equivalently, the fixed-completion route
3620   may establish continuation from a reflected rapidly decaying coefficient theta; its initial-half-plane
3621   Mellin identification is the compiled theorem CarrierTheta.theta_hasMellin_of_polynomial,
3622   while the global reflection of that same fixed-kernel theta is the remaining construction. On a

                                                            100
3623   neighbourhood supplied by one of these routes, the two sides of the claimed equation are analytic
3624   and agree on the axis, a set with accumulation points; by the identity theorem they agree identically.
3625   The dependency order is continuation → axis reality → functional equation → theta identity:
3626   with the residual extinct (Lemmas 62, 61) Mellin inversion returns the summed-bank self-duality
3627   𝐾 𝑟,𝜏 (1/𝑥) = 𝜀𝑟,𝜏 𝑥 𝜅 𝐾 𝑟,𝜏∨ (𝑥) as an output, which is what the Riemann–Hecke split of Prop. 57 (E) and
3628   the direct strip bound of Lemma 66 then consume — no step feeds on its successor.
3629        Why no Poisson — and why not termwise. Off the axis, 𝑥 ↦→ 1/𝑥 mixes distinct phasors: the
3630   reciprocal-height identity is a resummation across the bank, and per-phasor symmetry alone cannot
3631   supply it. Classically that resummation is Poisson/modularity — unavailable at 𝑟 ≥ 5. The route
3632   above never performs it: the inversion leg is used only on the axis, where it is conjugation, and
3633   continuation — a carrier property, not the fiber’s automorphy — carries it off. The 1D co-convergence
3634   gap ({Re 𝑠 > 𝜎0 } ∩ {Re 𝑠 < 𝜅 − 𝜎0 } empty for 𝜎0 > 𝜅/2) is the scalar chart’s record of the same
3635   fact: the half-plane series cannot reach the axis, so the classical frame must resummate; the carrier
3636   readout, continued to the axis by cell closure, need not.                                               □
3637   Axis reality is per-block Lean, whole-bank geometric (𝐽 with the balanced ledger), and machine-zero
3638   across the measured suite — Dirichlet Lean-complete, the Siegel (Sp(2𝑔, Z)) and Godement–Jacquet
3639   (GL(𝑟+1, Z)) carrier lattices, the twisted family through Sym13 and 𝐿(Sym5 Δ × 𝐸11 ) (§38, §39.1).

3718   39.1   The standard-side functional equation beyond the classical range: a carrier

3723   equation is the carrier’s own theta self-duality. We verify this standard-side functional equation

3752       The automorphy group carries the same signature. Sym𝑟 𝜋 lands on GL(𝑟+1), whose arithmetic
3753   group GL(𝑟+1, Z) is generated by the carrier’s own linear clocks {𝐸 𝑖𝑗 } together with the Poisson
3754   self-duality 𝜃(𝑌 −1 ) = det(𝑌)1/2 𝜃(𝑌) (the Godement–Jacquet matrix Fourier transform), verified
3755   to machine precision for 𝑛 = 𝑟+1 = 2, . . . , 7 — Sym1 through Sym6 , including GL(6) = Sym5
3756   (sym5_automorphy.py). This is the linear analogue of the symplectic tower Sp(2𝑔, Z) = (symmetric
3757   𝑔 × 𝑔 carrier clocks) + (Siegel-theta Poisson), the two laced by functoriality GSp(4) ↔ GL(4).
3758       We record the strength exactly: (8) is the standard-side (𝜏 trivial) functional equation, the
3759   Tate/Godement–Jacquet case, verified numerically at Sym5 . This computation does not itself
3760   address the twisted convolutions 𝐿(𝑠, Sym𝑟 𝜋 × 𝜏); those are treated structurally in Proposition 57
3761   by the reflection of the det-one tensor fiber.

3762   Direct test of the twisted objects. The structural treatment can now be checked head-on
3763   (twisted_cps_instance.py). As a factorizing control, the degree-12 fiber 𝐿(Sym5 Δ × Δ) — built
3764   on the carrier as a genuine twist — reproduces the standard-side product 𝐿(Sym6 Δ) 𝐿(Sym4 Δ)
3765   (Clebsch–Gordan Sym5 ⊗ Sym1 = Sym6 ⊕ Sym4 ) coefficientwise to 1.8 × 10−14 , validating the twisted
3766   pipeline against known quantities. The decisive run is non-factorizing: 𝐿(Sym5 Δ × 𝐸11 ), degree 12
3767   with two independent Satake angles 𝜃Δ , 𝜃𝐸 , does not reduce to symmetric powers of a single form —
3768   the exact shape Theorem 39 consumes past 𝑟 ≤ 4. Its carrier bank has no DC channel (every channel
3769   carries an odd 𝜃Δ -weight, so no total phase is identically zero), and the multi-rail closure tracks
3770   precision (4 × 10−28 at 30 digits, 9 × 10−88 at 90): the residual constant mode vanishes — entireness —
3771   on the twisted family itself, a first direct numerical instance of the converse theorem’s input beyond
3772   the classical range.


3773   40    Generalization: a representation-agnostic transport
3774   The construction is written for Sym𝑟 , but the symmetric-power pattern is nowhere used. This
3775   section isolates what the carrier actually consumes, exhibits the self-duality clock beneath the
3776   functional equation, and states the general transport with its two case-specific inputs.

3777   What the niceness argument uses. Re-read Proposition 57: the reflection pairs a weight channel
3778   𝑤 with its dual −𝑤; the det-one ledger is the balance of the ±𝑤 pairs; the completion is the two-clock
3779   Bessel (9) at the arbitrary shifts |𝑤|; boundedness and continuation are the two outputs of the warped-
3780   Abel representation, and entireness is the Riemann–Hecke continuation of the completed carrier theta
3781   once its finite zero-frequency residual modes are classified and shown to vanish (§39). None mentions
3782   the Chebyshev string {𝑟, 𝑟−2, . . . , −𝑟}. The carrier consumes only a finite weight multiset, its stability
3783   under 𝑤 ↦→ −𝑤, a modulus/determinant ledger, and the local factor det(1−𝑟(𝜑𝑣 (Frob𝑣 ))𝑞 𝑣−𝑠 )−1 . This

                                                              104
3784   is not a heuristic: it is the Lean theorem FiniteWeightFiber.localPoly_reciprocal (§39, App. B),
3785   which proves the ledger and the self-reciprocal local factor — the per-place functional equation
3786   — for any finite duality-stable weight multiset, with Sym𝑟 and Rankin–Selberg as instances. We
3787   also verify it numerically: for the non-Chebyshev Rankin–Selberg weight systems {±(𝑎+𝑏), ±(𝑎−𝑏)}
3788   of 𝐿( 𝑓 × 𝑔) ( 𝑓 , 𝑔 distinct level-one eigenforms; gaps not the uniform 2 of a symmetric power)
3789   the same completion closes the functional equation to machine precision (App. B). The genuine
3790   two-parameter instance 𝐿(Δ × 𝐸11 ) and the self-dual GL(3) = Sym2 of a real (Hejhal-computed)
3791   Maass form are worked in §31: the channel-resolved carrier closes both to precision, while the
3792   collapsed scalar readout degrades for the two-parameter object alone — a projection artifact, not a
3793   property of the fiber (gl4_rankin.py, gl3_maass_selfdual.py). The three-weight clock is not a
3794   new object: it is the two-clock composed with a third, (Bessel𝜇1 ,𝜇2 ) ★M clock𝜇3 , equal to the direct
       3-fold convolution by associativity and with Mellin 𝑖 ΓC (𝑠 + 𝜇𝑖 ) by the convolution theorem
                                                                Î
3795

3796   (App. B); and uniformity is additive, the trace bound ∥clockTraceN∥ ≤ 𝑛 being the sum of the
3797   pairwise two-clock bounds. Everything composes from the two-clock unit.

3798   The self-duality clock. The pairing 𝑤 ↦→ −𝑤, the reflection 𝑠 ↦→ 1 − 𝑠, the conjugation 𝑧 ↦→ 𝑧¯ ,
3799   and the Poisson 𝑆 : 𝜏 ↦→ −1/𝜏 (𝑆2 = −𝐼) are one order-two involution — the self-duality clock, the
3800   𝜇2 generator at scale 𝜋, beneath the 𝜇6 , 𝜇12 weight clocks in the harmonic ladder. Its tick is the
3801   functional equation; its fixed locus is Re 𝑠 = 12 (forced by the area law, scaleBalanced_iff); its
3802   cell is the phase step 𝜋 (the crossing spacing). The weight clocks are the channels it pairs; the
3803   self-duality clock is the pairing. This makes “duality-stable weight multiset” precise — a weight
3804   system closed under the 𝜇2 clock — and, being a structural involution, the clock is Galois-free: that
3805   is exactly why Sym𝑟 , Rankin–Selberg, and the Maass case (Corollary 47) close the same equation
3806   with only the channels changed.

3807   Ramified local data: the filtration tower. The carrier ingests not only the Satake class but the full
3808   Weil–Deligne datum (𝜌, 𝑁) at a ramified place; the raw local character becomes a clock-augmented
3809   local 𝐿- and 𝜀-factor. The monodromy 𝑁 is the 𝔰𝔩2 lowering ladder on the weight string (Steinberg
3810   Sp(𝑛) is the Sym𝑛−1 string with 𝑁 : 𝑤 ↦→ 𝑤 − 2), and 𝐿𝑣 = det(1 − Frob 𝑞 𝑣−𝑠 | (ker 𝑁)𝐼𝑣 )−1 reads
3811   Frobenius on the bottom of each ladder inside the inertia-invariants — as in the twist 𝐿(𝐸, Ad𝑔 ) at
3812   𝑝 = 13, where 𝐸 is Steinberg and the degree drops 2 → 1. The inertia is a root-of-unity clock: tame
                                                                                           𝑎/2
3813   inertia is a 𝜇𝑚 rotation, and the local root number is its Gauss sum 𝜀𝑣 = 𝜏(𝜒)/𝑞 𝑣 (|𝜀𝑣 | = 1, App. B).
3814   Wild inertia is the higher-ramification filtration as a tower 𝜇𝑝 ⊂ 𝜇𝑝 2 ⊂ · · · : the wild 𝜀-factor is the
3815   tower Gauss sum over (Z/𝑝 𝑎 )∗ , and it closes — |𝜀𝑣 | = 1 to 10−15 for conductor 𝑝 𝑎 (𝑎 ≤ 3, Swan ≤ 2),
3816   with the tower’s stationary phase reducing the wild sum to a single tame term keyed by the level-𝑎
3817   character (App. B). So the local dictionary is complete, tame and wild: 𝐿𝑣 from the monodromy
3818   ladder and inertia clock, 𝜀𝑣 from the filtration-tower Gauss sum.

3819   The content: the vanishing-adjustment clock. The layers so far — self-duality, completion,
3820   ramification — are the envelope: shared across a family, carrying no arithmetic. The content is
       a fourth clock. The raw object is the trivial-character series 𝜁(𝑠) = 𝑛 −𝑠 (all channels unit); the
                                                                              Í
3821

3822   Satake/Frobenius datum augments it by setting each phasor’s spin (the phase, the Satake angle
3823   𝜃𝑝 ) and magnitude (|𝑎 𝑛 |, bounded by Ramanujan), continuously in height and stepwise across
3824   primes as the carrier grows. The zeros are the focal cancellation of the adjusted bank — where the
3825   phasors align and sum to zero — located oracle-free by the growth scanner to 10−12 on Dirichlet,
3826   Δ, and 𝐸11 (Appendix B); the root number 𝜀 is the offset at the weld that places or doubles the
3827   central cancellation. Thus the clock-augmented 𝐿-function is the raw 𝜁 carried through four clock


                                                          105
3828   layers: self-duality (the 𝜇2 eta/theta envelope), completion (the two-clock Γ-shape), ramification
3829   (the inertia/monodromy clocks), and this vanishing-adjustment clock (the arithmetic, as phasor
3830   spin and magnitude producing the zeros). The content is not opaque — it is the layer that turns
3831   Satake data into vanishing — though it is fed that data; the clock operates the arithmetic, it does not
3832   conjure it.

3833   The vanishing clock in the Hodge substructure: signature-based cycle detection. The following is
3834   preliminary: a calibration that opened a separate development, the loss-ledger ↔ cycle-filtration correspondence
3835   sketched in §44 and deferred to a companion paper. The completion clock is already the Hodge realization
3836   — ΓC (𝑠 + 𝜇) is the Hodge type (𝑝, 𝑞) with 𝑝 − 𝑞 = 2𝜇 — so the dimension clock projects into a Hodge
3837   structure by construction. Paired with the vanishing clock it reads the algebraic substructure through
3838   the Beilinson–Bloch vanishing–cycle-rank correspondence: in the theorem-anchored instances
3839   below (the identity 𝑟(𝐸, Ad𝑔 ) = rank 𝐸(𝑀) − rank 𝐸(𝑄) of §36.2 and the |Sha| ladder of §37), central
3840   vanishing order agrees with the corresponding cycle multiplicity, while the general correspondence
3841   is deferred to the companion paper; and algebraicity itself is detected by the vanishing signature,
3842   not a single special value. Two instances, both measured (App. B). CM: the (1, 1) class of Sym2 𝐸 is
3843   algebraic iff 𝐸 has complex multiplication, and the clock reads it off the 𝑎 𝑝 -signature — a CM curve
3844   has 𝑎 𝑝 = 0 at every inert prime (399/399 for 𝑦 2 = 𝑥 3 − 𝑥 over Q(𝑖); 4/399 for the non-CM 37𝑎), the
3845   𝜇2 clock of the CM field marking the symmetric-square pole. Twist-correspondence: given 𝑓 and
3846   a form 𝑔 that is secretly 𝑓 ⊗ 𝜒5 (unequal coefficients), the Rankin–Selberg pole signature — the
3847   DC-residue slope of 𝐿( 𝑓 × 𝑔 ⊗ 𝜓) scanned over 𝜓 — surfaces the hidden algebraic Tate class in
3848   𝐻 1 ( 𝑓 ) ⊗ 𝐻 1 (𝑔 ⊗ 𝜒5 ) at 𝜓 = 𝜒5 (slope 0.71 against ≤ 0.04 elsewhere), with an unrelated control flat at
3849   every 𝜓. The core detection (Rankin–Selberg poles marking twist-equivalence) is classical; what the
3850   clock adds is the unified reading — the vanishing clock’s signature inside the Hodge projection,
3851   one detector — and the dynamical scan that surfaces a correspondence rather than confirming a
3852   known one. Recursive tower: the same signature climbs the symmetric-power tower. The pole order
3853   of 𝐿(Sym𝑟 𝑓 × Sym𝑟 𝑓 ) is the count of algebraic self-correspondences at level 𝑟 — the multiplicity of
3854   the trivial in Sym𝑟 ⊗ Sym𝑟 as a Sato–Tate representation. For a generic form it is 1 at every level
3855   (Sym𝑟 irreducible under SU(2)); for a CM form it climbs 1, 2, 2, 3, · · · = ⌈(𝑟+1)/2⌉, the extra cycles of
3856   𝑁(𝑈(1)) appearing level by level. Measured (App. B): the DC-residue   √            slope tower is flat for the
3857   non-CM 37𝑎 and climbs identically for CM over Q(𝑖) and Q( −3), the CM/non-CM ratio tracking
3858   1, 2, 2, 3. The pole orders themselves are the Sato–Tate moments (classical); what the clock supplies
3859   is the recursive reading of the cycle tower, level by level, distinguishing the Sato–Tate/Hodge
3860   structure from the signature alone.
3861        Calibration (what these preliminaries opened). Pushing the reading toward the layers invisible to
3862   ordinary Hodge projection — homologically-trivial cycles, the Abel–Jacobi kernel, filtration depth
3863   — one asks whether each is carried by a distinct retained carrier coordinate. The leading central
       jet factors, by the BSD/Gross–Zagier formula [23, 24] 𝐿(𝑟) (𝐸, 1)/𝑟! = Ω · Reg · |Sha| · 𝑝 𝑐 𝑝 /𝑇 2 ,

3866   order 𝑟 (vanishing multiplicity), the regulator Reg (the height/Abel–Jacobi datum), and |Sha|
3867   (the local–global obstruction) — e.g. order 0 with |Sha| ∈ {1, 4, 9} and |Sha| = 1 with order
3868   ∈ {1, 2, 3} at distinct Reg. So three filtration layers do get three distinct coordinates. The semisimple

3874   class — the modified diagonal in CH2 (𝐶 3 )0 — is the tensor-cube test case, where theorem-anchored

3879   The reflection is carrier geometry; the FE clock adapts it. The functional equation is not an analytic
3880   hypothesis on the fiber but a property of the carrier geometry: the helix–anti-helix conjugation,
3881   fixed at Re 𝑠 = 12 , is the natural functional equation, proven per-place (localPoly_reciprocal) and
3882   invariant under the dual-compatible unit warps (warpFiber). Whether every warp preserves it we
3883   do not assert — and we do not need to, because that is exactly what the FE clock is for. When
3884   the natural reflection already closes (the self-dual, aligned case) the clock is inert. When a warp
3885   perturbs the closure, or when 𝑟 is not self-dual — so the reflection pairs 𝐿(𝑠, 𝑟 ◦ 𝜑) with 𝐿(𝑠, 𝑟 ∨ ◦ 𝜑)
3886   — a tunable FE clock/adapter is switched in to restore it: at its simplest the 𝜇2 self-duality clock
3887   doubling onto 𝑟 ⊕ 𝑟 ∨ , whose weight system {𝑤} ∪ {−𝑤} is closed under 𝑤 ↦→ −𝑤 by construction
3888   so that 𝐿(𝑠, (𝑟 ⊕ 𝑟 ∨ ) ◦ 𝜑) = 𝐿(𝑠, 𝑟 ◦ 𝜑) 𝐿(𝑠, 𝑟 ∨ ◦ 𝜑) carries a genuine self-dual functional equation;
3889   more generally the clock’s phase and scale are tuned to the fiber’s own weight ledger. So the
3890   natural reflection is geometric and free, and FE closure never rests on universal warp-invariance:
3891   the tunable adapter supplies whatever adjustment a given warp requires.

3892   The general transport, and its two inputs. The analytic side is thus representation-agnostic:
3893   functional equation (the carrier reflection), completion (two-clock), and — from the one carrier-cell
3894   theorem (exact zero cell mean of the adapted warp) — continuation, vertical bound, and entireness
3895   hold for every finite duality-stable weight system, uniformly in 𝑟. The transport itself needs nothing
3896   further: it consumes an admissible function — the finite placewise presentation of Definition 5 —
3897   directly, with no local-Langlands datum. Two case-specific steps enter only the classical naming
3898   of the output as 𝑟∗ (𝜋) automorphic on GL𝑁 , neither Sym𝑟 -special: (i) local Langlands for the
3899   source 𝐺 — a translation step, not a system input — to source the admissible presentation from an
3900   automorphic 𝜋 (producing 𝜑𝑣 and the local factors) and to identify the output classically; free for
3901   GL2 (symmetric powers, Rankin–Selberg), a theorem in many cases in general; and (ii) the converse
3902   theorem into GL𝑁 [14], which promotes the nice 𝐿-function to an automorphic form, and whose
3903   twisted-niceness input is again a duality-stable warp the carrier supplies. Within these, Sym𝑟 was
3904   the first nontrivial clock family the carrier consumed, not the mechanism: on the analytic side the
3905   carrier is a representation-agnostic Langlands-transport engine.

3906   Harmonization: the transform dictionary, and the method as its own proof. The whole process
3907   — reading a function, letting its nature name the frame it requires, and enlarging or warping the
3908   carrier to that frame so the function closes — is one we call harmonization, after its classical archetype:
3909   a class-group obstruction is an untranslated frame mismatch that dissolves the moment the carrier
3910   is enlarged to the field the obstruction itself names (capitulation; Furtwängler’s Principal Ideal
3911   Theorem). The function’s nature selects its adapter — one does not pick a universal transform
3912   and hope. And those adapters are, place by place, the established machinery of the Satake–Hecke
3913   picture, re-read. The self-duality clock is the Weyl group acting on the dual torus (for GL(2),
3914   𝛼 ↔ 𝛼−1 ), so a duality-stable weight multiset is a Weyl orbit and the carrier’s duality is built
3915   in; the centering to Re 𝑠 = 12 is the 𝜌-shift 𝛿1/2 ; the completion that assembles the local factor
3916   is Macdonald’s spherical-function formula / the Harish-Chandra 𝑐-function, a Weyl sum over
3917   the orbit; the local factor det(1 − 𝑟(𝐴)𝑞 −𝑠 )−1 is the Satake transform through 𝑟; and the reading


                                                          107
3918   measure is Plancherel. A cuspidal fiber’s function warp is a chart-conversion clock that rationalises
3919   its data: passing from the multiplicative Satake angle to the completely additive prime-count
3920   winding Θ(𝑛) = (𝜋/3)Ω(𝑛) turns the carrier phase into a root of unity 𝛽 Ω(𝑛) (𝛽 = 𝑒 𝑖 𝑘𝜋/3 ) — a
3921   Liouville-type completely multiplicative twist, whatever the (irrational) Satake angle — and the
3922   warp exp(𝑖𝜀 sin 𝑘Θ) is, by Jacobi–Anger, a Bessel-weighted superposition of these root-of-unity
3923   twists (carrier_warp_check.py, carrier_lockin.py), its cell closing by the classical vanishing of
       the Liouville-type mean, 𝑛≤𝑋 𝛽 Ω(𝑛) = 𝑜(𝑋). The claim is in fact universal, only not enumerated:
                                    Í
3924

3925   for every fiber there exists an adapter, selected by the fiber’s own nature, under which it closes —
3926   an ∀∃ statement, not one transform imposed on all — and its archetype, capitulation, is already
3927   a universal theorem (every ideal becomes principal in the frame it names). What we decline is
3928   the enumeration of every (function, adapter) pair. The method is established the way such a
3929   method is: a few representative classes are proved outright (the finite duality-stable harmonic
3930   fibers and the Dirichlet family, in Lean, §39), and a substantial subset of the dictionary is itself
3931   machine-checked rather than merely numerical — the two-clock completion and weight law
3932   (TwoClockWeightLaw: two_clock_weight, ramanujan_line_ceiling, dc_offset), the jet/rank
3933   clock (BSDClocks: rank_is_dc_residue, leading_jet_extraction, gz_first_jet_live), the
3934   arithmetic clock and gauge gap
3935   (ClockStructure: arithmetic_clock_law, gauge_gap_law, obstruction_recovery), the clock–
3936   dip lock-in
3937   (ClockDipDuality: locked_dips_add, unlocked_dips_cancel), the reflection (FiniteWeightFiber),
3938   and the cell closure (CellClosure); the adapters that close the remaining cases are named and
3939   grounded in existing theory (the dictionary above, necessarily partial — some adapters were built
3940   and never needed); and the per-fiber architecture makes the universal principle operative rather
3941   than aspirational — a fiber outside the proved classes engages its own adapter, and a resistant fiber
3942   is diagnostic rather than automatically fatal.
3943       We fully expect novel inputs to expose adapter forms not yet named in the paper. A resistant
3944   fiber either identifies missing structural data in the stated presentation, or exhibits failure of the
3945   synthesized carrier-closure condition; in the latter case it is a counterexample to universality on
3946   the declared source class. This fixes what a genuine counterexample must be. It is not enough
3947   to exhibit a fiber that the present dictionary does not close; a real counterexample must exhibit
3948   a payload for which no harmonization consistent with its intrinsic dynamics can satisfy the carrier and
3949   ledger laws while preserving faithful readout. That is the falsifiable content of the universal claim, and it
3950   is the burden a disconfirmation must meet.

3951   The operational adapter suite. The dictionary above is place-by-place; what operates it is a suite of
3952   three adapters, each keyed to the measured transport clock, that the carrier switches in to close a
3953   readout the raw projection smears (introduced in §30; named here as a unit).
3954 (1) The clock configurator reads the deterministic transport frequency 𝜈clock = 2𝜈𝐽 off the orbital
3955     transform (𝑅2 = 1.000, §30) and sets the period, phase, and scale the other three inherit. It repairs
3956     nothing itself — it configures: identifying the clock is necessary but not sufficient.
3957 (2) The carrier dwell re-registers the values a projected sum skips — the fiber takes a siding whose

3958     length is the height offset, traverses the omitted lattice points, and returns to the same carrier
3959     position with its phasors re-aligned. This is the native, exact form of Altuğ’s Σ() missing-lattice-
3960     point correction (3400× closure contrast against the cut track, §31, skip_insert_closure.py).
                                                                             2       1
3961 (3) The phasor delay adapter, derived from the clock (slope 𝑏 = −1/𝑥 , 𝑥 0 =
                                                                             0       2 log 𝑁, not fit), retards
3962     the faster-spinning higher-weight channels so a single-rail Chebyshev bank does not over-rotate
3963     within a dwell period. On the Sym𝑟 tower it raises the reopening exponent partially (𝑘 : 0.48 → 0.61


                                                          108
3964      at 𝑟 = 13 in the delay experiment dwell_retard.py, whose 0.48 baseline is that experiment’s
3965      setup, distinct from the 0.44 full-readout smear of the §31 table); a single delay is a one-rail
3966      correction, and a genuinely multi-parameter fiber is closed instead by the channel-resolved
3967      (multi-rail) readout of §31, not by a scalar delay.
3968   The clock configurator selects; the other three execute — period, registration, spin, dissipation.
3969   This is the operational face of harmonization: the fiber’s nature, read through the clock, names the
3970   adapters it needs.


3971   41    The transport machine and universal carrier transport
3972   Exotic adapters: the parallel-dimension clock. The clocks above act on one carrier. A transfer
3973   between two automorphic worlds — a functorial lift 𝑟 : 𝐿 𝐺 → 𝐿 𝐻, a theta correspondence, a base
3974   change — is, in this language, a parallel-dimension clock: it absorbs the local state on the source
3975   carrier, reflects it onto an alternate carrier (the target 𝐿 𝐻, or an auxiliary object such as the Weil
3976   representation or an Eisenstein series) that runs its own clock system, applies the transfer there, and
3977   reflects the result back. The archetype is the theta correspondence, where the Weil representation
3978   on the metaplectic cover is such an alternate helix, and the GSp(4) ↔ GL(4) lacing of §38 is one
3979   instance already used. A non-theta instance goes through uniformly on the carrier: quadratic base
3980   change Δ ↦→ Δ𝐸 over 𝐸 = Q(𝑖) — reflect Δ onto the carrier over 𝐸 (the base-change Satake: split
3981   𝑝 giving two channels, inert 𝑝 the Frobenius-squared channel) and reflect back through the 𝜒−4
3982   clock, the factorization 𝐿(Δ𝐸 , 𝑠) = 𝐿(Δ, 𝑠)𝐿(Δ ⊗ 𝜒−4 , 𝑠) — reproduces the base-change Satake exactly
3983   and closes the reflected degree-four functional equation on the equal-shift two-clock 𝐾0 to 10−26
3984   (App. B). Because the alternate carrier may itself carry parallel-dimension clocks, the construction is
3985   recursive — the functoriality web as a tower of reflections. The mechanism is thus not a metaphor:
3986   base change (reducible), Sym𝑟 (irreducible), and theta (dual pair) are three worked instances.
3987   Isolation note. The universal transport arrows consumed below are isolated in Part I: car-
3988   rier/involution in §2, residual dictionary in §7, readout and reflection in §7, and coherent composition
3989   in §8. The theorem below keeps the transported Satake/tensor specialization.

4023   rule, not by its values. The placewise assignment 𝑣 ↦→ 𝐴𝑣 (𝑊) is required to be generated by a finite rule —
4024   a finite parameter set or effective structural schema fixed independently of how many places are queried, not a
4025   place-by-place list; thus finite structural presentation refers to finite description complexity of the source law,
4026   not merely finite local dimension at each place. A source carrying no such law — a structureless (“random”)
4027   function whose only faithful description is its own sample path — is not admissible: there is no finite structure
4028   from which to synthesize a carrier phase, a native cell, or a clock, and letting an adapter encode the sample

4072   cancellation needs; restoring the omitted coordinates makes the phase gaugeable and names the
4073   correct cell, which is adapter synthesis from a determinate finite law.
4074        Falsifiable content. Because the load-bearing input is the per-fiber cell closure, the universal claim
4075   is falsifiable at a single point: a genuine counterexample is not a fiber the dictionary has merely not yet
4076   been run on, but a fiber 𝑊 for which no harmonization consistent with its intrinsic dynamics closes
4077   its cells while satisfying the carrier and ledger laws and preserving faithful readout. The ∀∃ shape —
4078   for every 𝑊 a matched, cell-closing adapter suite exists — is the universal content, and it is proved
4079   in closed form, not sampled: any nonzero cell residual is forcible to zero once two R-independent
4080   directions span C (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible, Lean), and a continuous non-constant
4081   lane phase supplies the independent pair (CarrierReachability.reachable_independent_stage,
4082   Lean), the two composed by direct application — so the enumeration of every (𝑊 , suite) pair
4083   is not required. The general family (Sym13 , the two-parameter 𝐿(Δ × 𝐸11 ), the genuine twisted
4084   𝐿(Sym5 Δ×𝐸11 ), the real Maass Sym2 ; §31) is the set of instances where we additionally ran empirical
4085   checks — calibration and independent reproduction at the float floor, not the basis of the claim. Two
4086   boundaries bound the claim: within admissibility, the theorem’s own hypothesis — the independent
4087   pair, a non-degenerate warp Jacobian read from the law — which every synthesized fiber to date
4088   satisfies; outside admissibility, a structureless source has no law to synthesize from and is the
4089   limiting non-example, the point at which description complexity has become the state.

4090   Corollary 78 (Simultaneous carrier synchronization). The transport is universal not only fiberwise but
4091   for simultaneous synchronization. Let 𝑊1 , . . . , 𝑊𝑚 be admissible sources — each a function (or Hodge
4092   datum) realized as a 3D carrier+fiber pair and closing its cells exactly by (c); native cell scales, ranks, phase
4093   conventions, clock laws, and dimensional realizations may differ. Then a per-source normalization augments

                                                             111
4094   both halves of each pair — the carrier (its cell scale and clock chart) and the fiber (the function’s warp and
4095   weight chart) — bringing each to a carrier+fiber form mutually compatible with the others on one common
4096   carrier, so the transported sources     evolve and are read simultaneously: the unified readout is the tuple
       Q(𝜏) = 𝑄 1# (𝜏), . . . , 𝑄 𝑚
                                  # (𝜏) , recording exact coordinatewise closures. Each fiber remains distinct and keeps
                                       
4097

4098   its own focal-closure events — a source vanishing of 𝑊𝑗 is an exact zero of 𝑄 #𝑗 at a harmonic cell boundary,
4099   with no uncancelled cell remainder — and the fibers need not share native ordinates, cell scales, or clocks.

4100       The synchronization obligation. The one requirement beyond the fiberwise closures is that the
4101   normalization preserve exact boundary closure — carry each exact cell closure to an exact cell closure
4102   on the common carrier — not merely align zero locations. This holds by construction for the
4103   harmonized (root-of-unity) normalization, where the 𝜇𝑀 snap sends every channel to a shared
4104   cell and the joint bank closes coordinatewise (§31), and is validated on the genuine two-fiber case
4105   𝐿(Δ × 𝐸11 ): its two rails synchronize on one carrier and close jointly to 4.9 × 10−91 (gl4_rankin.py).
4106   As in Theorem 77 this is exact closure on the carrier bank, not an analytic-residue claim.
4107   Isolation note. The source-independent synchronization and common-refinement obligation from
4108   Corollary 78 is isolated in §5. The numerical two-fiber and root-of-unity checks remain here as
4109   source/application evidence.

4110   Corollary 79 (Universal functoriality in rank). Theorem 77 carries every admissible fiber faithfully, its
4111   reflection and local data unconditional and its niceness the cell-closure output; that output is uniform in rank,
4112   for the construction refers nowhere to the degree 𝑁, the source group 𝐺, or the symmetric-power string: the
4113   reflection (localPoly_reciprocal), the two-clock completion, the warped-Abel continuation and vertical
4114   bound, and the Riemann–Hecke entireness (the one carrier-cell theorem) are stated for an arbitrary finite
4115   duality-stable weight system, uniformly in rank. For objects on GL(2) data the two remaining ingredients
4116   are standing theorems, not hypotheses: local Langlands for GL(2) furnishes 𝜑𝜋,𝑣 and the local factors at every
4117   place, and the converse theorem into GL𝑁 [14] promotes a nice 𝐿-function to an automorphic form. What
4118   neither classically controls at every rank — the twisted niceness of 𝐿(𝑟 ◦ 𝜑𝜋 × 𝜏) for all 𝜏, entire and bounded
4119   and self-dual — is exactly what the carrier discharges, uniformly in rank. Consequently, every finite duality-
4120   stable weight system 𝑟 on GL(2) data transfers: feeding the carrier’s nice datum into the GL𝑁 converse
4121   theorem — discharged place-by-place as the explicit hypothesis ledger of Part III (Theorem 42, Corollary 43)
4122   — makes 𝑟 ◦ 𝜑𝜋 automorphic on GL𝑁 , cuspidal for non-exceptional 𝜋 and isobaric for the finitely many
4123   exceptional types (§16), uniformly in rank and degree: the full symmetric-power tower and the Rankin–Selberg
4124   weight systems {±(𝑎 ± 𝑏)} alike. The low-degree cases recover known functoriality, as they must — Sym2
4125   (Gelbart–Jacquet [6]), Sym3 , Sym4 (Kim–Shahidi [17]), the classical convolution lifts; the content is that the
4126   same mechanism continues past the Langlands–Shahidi range (𝑟 ≥ 5) with no new ingredient, the niceness
4127   being carrier-discharged rather than Eisenstein-constructed. Scope. The niceness argument’s Lean theorems
4128   are stated at the general interface, not for particular functions, and they generalize automatically because they
4129   read only the fiber’s abstract data: the per-place reflection holds for any finite duality-stable weight multiset
4130   (FiniteWeightFiber.localPoly_reciprocal); the completed-reflection assembly carries no Dirichlet
4131   hypothesis (FiniteWeightFiber.symTensorCompleted_FE, any 𝑟, any unit twist); the entireness mecha-
4132   nism is channel-agnostic in (𝐴, 𝐵, 𝜇, 𝜆) (HarmonicCell.harmonic_residual_no_independent_mode);
4133   and cell closure is the closed-form forcibility above (ForcibleClosure.residual_forcible). The har-
4134   monic and Dirichlet classes are therefore end-to-end instantiations of general proofs, not the proofs’ boundary,
4135   and the general family (Sym13 , 𝐿(Δ × 𝐸11 ), the genuine twisted 𝐿(Sym5 Δ × 𝐸11 ), real Maass Sym2 ; §31) is
4136   instance calibration. No local-Langlands datum is required by the transport itself — the carrier consumes the
4137   admissible presentation directly (Definition 5); for a source group beyond GL(2), local Langlands at that
4138   group enters only to source that presentation from a classical 𝜋 and to name the output — a translation step,
4139   a theorem in many cases, not a system dependence.


                                                             112
4140   Remark 80 (Universality and functoriality are distinct claims). Isolation note. The general coherence
4141   laws in this remark are the Part I transport obligations recorded in §8; the symmetric-power, tensor,
4142   and base-change instances stay here as applications.
4143        Two claims here should not be conflated. Universality is the existence of compatible carrier
4144   realizations (Cor. 78): any finite collection of exact-closing source fibers admits source-dependent
4145   normalizations 𝒩𝐹 placing them on one common carrier, run and read simultaneously with exact
4146   focal closure preserved — universal by normalization, compatible by carrier realization, no shared native
4147   representation required. That is theorem-level here.
4148        Functoriality is the separate coherence law on structural maps between sources: a transport
4149    𝑓 : 𝐹 → 𝐺 should induce a carrier transport 𝑓b with 𝒩𝐺 ◦ 𝑓 ≃ 𝑓b ◦ 𝒩𝐹 (naturality), the identity
4150   inducing the identity, 𝑔  ◦ 𝑓 ≃𝑔
                                       b◦ b𝑓 (composition), and exact focal closure preserved — where ≃ is
4151   a declared carrier equivalence (chart reparameterization, phase conjugacy, block permutation, not
4152   exact equality) and the normalizations need not be unique. For the explicit transports of this paper
4153   — symmetric power, Rankin–Selberg tensor, base change — naturality and faithfulness hold because
4154
       b𝑓 is the same weight-system operation on the normalized bank that 𝑓 is on the source. Identity and
4155   composition, the decisive tests, are verified: at the weight-system level 𝑊id = id and 𝑊𝑟◦𝑠 = 𝑊𝑟 ◦ 𝑊𝑠 ,
4156   each composite an exact disjoint union of irreducible blocks (the plethysm — Sym2 ◦ Sym2 =
4157   Sym4 ⊕ Sym0 , Sym3 ◦ Sym3 = Sym9 ⊕ Sym5 ⊕ Sym3 — coherent up to the block permutation in ≃),
4158   tensor and base change composing likewise (composition_test.py); and the coherence laws are
4159   machine-checked — associativity, two-sided identity, base-change composition bc𝑝 ◦ bc𝑞 = bc𝑝𝑞 , and
4160   preservation of exact focal closure under composition (CarrierFunctoriality). For the CPS tower
4161   this coherence is instantiated on the genuine Satake-bank state, with strict equality 𝑇𝑔 ℎ = 𝑇𝑔 ◦ 𝑇ℎ and
4162   exact bank-zero preservation (ThreeDConverse.cpsTowerFunctoriality3D_unified); no carrier
4163   equivalence is needed in that instance. The carrier-equivalence formulation is retained only
4164   for structural transports between arbitrary source presentations whose native charts differ. The
4165   Langlands functoriality of Cor. 79 is the arithmetic instance this coherence delivers, not a separate
4166   mechanism. In one line: the carrier is universal for simultaneous harmonic realization, and functorial
4167   with respect to those source transports that commute, up to carrier equivalence, with faithful harmonic
4168   normalization.


4169   Part VI
4170   Other Significant Results
4171   42    Obstruction-directed harmonization: from detection to removal
4172   The transport of Theorem 77 is, so far, an obstruction detector and locator: it reads a source, and
4173   where a mode fails to close it names the obstruction coordinate 𝛼 = Obs(𝑋) ≠ 0 and, through the
4174   tower, the finite depth at which it lives — the ledger certifying that 𝛼 was carried, not discarded.
4175   The capitulation archetype above shows the next arrow: an obstruction can dissolve once the carrier
4176   is enlarged to the frame its own signature names. We record that arrow as an operator and state the
4177   general removal as a target, guarded by an explicit killability boundary.

4178   Remark 81 (The obstruction-directed extension operator). Given a carrier state 𝒞 and a detected
4179   obstruction 𝛼 = Obs(𝒞) ≠ 0 — a persistent non-closing mode, localized to a finite tower depth —




                                                         113
4180   the obstruction-directed extension

                                              𝔈 : (𝒞, 𝛼) ↦−→ (𝒞𝛼 , 𝜄 𝛼 , ℎ 𝛼 )

4181   returns a faithful transport 𝜄 𝛼 : 𝒞 → 𝒞𝛼 (preserving readout and the ledger laws) and a primitive
4182   ℎ 𝛼 with
                                          𝑑 ℎ 𝛼 = 𝜄 𝛼∗ (𝛼), so   [𝜄 𝛼∗ 𝛼] = 0
4183   in the source-relevant cohomology of 𝒞𝛼 : the transported cocycle becomes a coboundary. The
4184   extension data are determined by the signature of 𝛼, not found by search — the non-closing mode
4185   names the missing carrier coordinate, harmonization synthesizes it (the constructive Synth of
4186   Theorem 77, now applied to the extension), and exact focal closure in 𝒞𝛼 is the witness 𝑑ℎ 𝛼 = 𝛼# , a
4187   genuine null-homotopy rather than a vanished scalar readout. The framework thus reads

         Detect (𝛼 ≠ 0) → Localize (signature, depth) → Harmonize away 𝛼 ↦→ (𝒞𝛼 , ℎ 𝛼 ), 𝑑ℎ 𝛼 = 𝛼#
                                                                                                           


4188   with certificate the pair (𝒞𝛼 , ℎ 𝛼 ) and its focal-closure witness.

4189   The proven prototype: capitulation. Furtwängler’s Principal Ideal Theorem is 𝔈 for the ideal-class
4190   obstruction. The signature is a nonprincipal class 𝛼 ∈ Cl(𝐾); the extension 𝒞𝛼 is the Hilbert class
4191   field 𝐻, the frame 𝛼 itself names; 𝜄 𝛼 is extension of scalars 𝐾 ↩→ 𝐻; and the primitive ℎ 𝛼 is the
4192   principal generator that appears there, [𝜄 𝛼∗ 𝛼] = 0 being capitulation (every ideal becomes principal
4193   in 𝐻). The signature determines the extension and the witness is constructed, not assumed — a
4194   proven instance of the operator, already universal in its own domain (every class capitulates in the
4195   class field it names).

4196   A second, adversarial prototype: the Brauer-zero trap. Detection and removal separate most
4197   sharply where the aggregate readout already closes. Take the Hamilton class [𝐴], 𝐴 = (−1, −1)Q ∈
       Br(Q): global reciprocity forces its local invariants to sum to zero, 𝑣 inv𝑣 (𝐴) = 12 + 12 ≡ 0 in
                                                                                    Í
4198

4199   Q/Z, so every scalar/global reading is harmonically closed — yet [𝐴] ≠ 0, the invariant vector
4200   (inv2 , inv∞ ) = ( 21 , 12 ) being nonzero. A detector that equated a closed readout with a killed class
4201   would false-positive here; the ledger instead retains the vector. Run blind, the controller given
4202   no splitting field, 𝔈 (A) detects the retained obstruction despite the zero sum, (B) classifies it as
4203   2-torsion ramified at {2, ∞}, (C) synthesizes from that syndrome√         alone a finite chart with even
4204   local degree at those places — the minimal being 𝐾 = Q( −3), not supplied and not the textbook
                                                                 ′

4205   Q(𝑖), (D) removes: a direct Brauer computation confirms res𝐾′/Q [𝐴] = 0, and (E) certifies 𝑅(𝑋 # ) = 0
4206   and Obs(𝑋 # ) = 0 together — the conjunction detection alone cannot supply. That the√repair is
4207   synthesized, not hard-coded, is forced by a second class ramified at {3, 5}: a fixed “adjoin −1” rule
4208   splits Hamilton but cannot split it, while the syndrome search repairs both (brauer_zero_trap.py,
4209   every stage checked against the classical Brauer/Hilbert-symbol oracle). The five passes — detect
4210   / classify / synthesize / remove / certify, run with no target field in the adapter library and
4211   charged for extension degree — are the test methodology; the removal logic they enforce is machine-
       checked in Lean: that a zero aggregate never counts as removal ( 𝑣 inv𝑣 = 0 does not force the
