4214   a 2-torsion class (removal), and that the certificate is the conjunction aggregate = 0 ∧ vector = 0
4215   (certified_removal) — BrauerZeroTrap.lean. Brauer classes over a number field are, moreover,
4216   a regime where the killability boundary is provably met: by the global theory of central simple
4217   algebras over number fields — Albert–Brauer–Hasse–Noether together with the cyclicity theorem


                                                           114
4218   — every class admits a finite cyclic splitting extension, so the terminating-signature condition holds
4219   group-wide, and the benchmark supplies the constructive syndrome-directed synthesis for the
4220   2-torsion (quaternionic) part. The general finite-depth characterization, beyond Brauer, remains the
4221   target above.

4222   What is already in hand. The detection side is machine-checked: the obstruction is a well-
4223   defined measured coordinate (GeneralizedCohomology: DistinguishedPoint, obstruction_eq,
4224   measurement_sound, the tower reading 𝛼 exactly), and faithful transport preserves closure under
4225   composition (CarrierFunctoriality.faithful_comp, no axioms), so a nullification once achieved
4226   is carried by any further functorial transport. What 𝔈 adds beyond detection is the witness ℎ 𝛼 ; the
4227   depth at which to build it is supplied by the delayed tower signature (first-nonzero tower depth =
4228   filtration depth, §44).

4229   Obstruction-directed harmonization (target). We state the general removal as the frontier this
4230   opens, evidence-weighed, not as a proved result: for a finite-depth obstruction signature detected by
4231   the carrier tower, the signature determines — by a computable synthesis rule, up to carrier equivalence
4232   — a finite harmonizing extension 𝒞𝛼 and a primitive ℎ 𝛼 with 𝑑ℎ 𝛼 = 𝜄 𝛼∗ 𝛼, so the transported obstruction
4233   is exact, the nullification witnessed by complete focal closure and preserved under functorial transport.
4234   Version 1 asks only existence plus a computable rule, not canonicity. The supporting evidence is the
4235   capitulation prototype, the constructive Synth operator, and the finite depth index of the tower; and
4236   the termination half is no longer wholly open — it is characterized below by a local–global principle
4237   at the signature’s depth (Proposition 82), unconditional at depths 1 and 2, the non-terminating
4238   boundary being the stably essential classes (not removable by finite enlargement). What remains is
4239   the local–global principle at higher depth and the synthesis rule off the two settled regimes.

4240   Killability boundary, and what would falsify it. The claim is guarded, and pre-commits to its
4241   failure modes. (1) Visibility does not imply killability: not every detected class is removable by a finite
4242   extension; a class that stays nonzero under every permitted finite extension is outside scope, and
4243   characterizing the signatures for which the synthesis terminates is the open content, not a defect. (2)
4244   No arbitrary enlargement: the extension must be named by the signature (as capitulation’s class field
4245   is named by the class); enlarging blindly until the readout vanishes is oracular and vacuous — the
4246   structureless boundary of Theorem 77 again. (3) A real coboundary, not a zero readout: exact focal
4247   closure must certify 𝑑ℎ 𝛼 = 𝛼# in the source-relevant cohomology, a genuine null-homotopy, with
4248   the ledger proving 𝛼 was carried, not thrown away; a vanished scalar symptom without a witness
4249   does not count. (4) Finite depth: the extension is built at the tower depth the signature reports, so a
4250   terminating synthesis is finite. A disconfirmation — a finitely-presented, finite-depth signature
4251   that its own named frame extension provably cannot make exact — would falsify the target, and
4252   would be published as prominently as a confirmation; none is known.

4253   The reach of the operator: a local–global characterization. Which signatures terminate is not left
4254   open in the mass; it is organized by one principle. A finite-depth signature 𝛼 is removable by a
4255   finite carrier extension exactly when a local–global principle holds for it at its detection depth 𝑑: 𝛼
4256   capitulates in a finite cover precisely when it is locally trivial — killed under restriction to every
4257   completion of the carrier. Capitulation and the Brauer splitting are then not two coincidences but
4258   the depth-1 and depth-2 instances of one mechanism, and both are unconditional.
4259   Proposition 82 (Terminating signatures: two unconditional regimes). Let 𝐺 be the carrier’s structure
4260   group and 𝑀 finite coefficients. (a) Every depth-1 signature terminates. A continuous class 𝛼 ∈ 𝐻 1 (𝐺, 𝑀)

                                                          115
4261   is inflated from a finite quotient 𝐺/𝑈, so by inflation–restriction res𝑈 𝛼 = res𝑈 inf 𝛼¯ = 0: 𝛼 dies in the
4262   finite cover 𝒞𝑈 . This is capitulation — for ideal classes, Furtwängler’s Principal Ideal Theorem. (b) Every
4263   Brauer (𝐻 2 ) signature over a global carrier terminates, by the global theory of central simple algebras over
4264   number fields — Albert–Brauer–Hasse–Noether together with the cyclicity theorem: the vanishing of the
4265   summed local invariants (reciprocity) forces a finite cyclic splitting extension. The constructive synthesis for
4266   the 2-torsion part is the Brauer-zero trap (brauer_zero_trap.py, BrauerZeroTrap.lean).
4267   The boundary is equally sharp: termination fails exactly where the local–global principle fails
4268   at depth 𝑑 — for a stably essential class, one nonzero under restriction to every finite admissible
4269   carrier enlargement and therefore not removable by finite enlargement. The boundary beyond
4270   the terminating local–global regimes is not identified here with the transcendental Griffiths group.
4271   Detection is a separate question from removal: finite-tower visibility of Griffiths/Ceresa extension
4272   data depends on the joint faithfulness of the derivative/height tower and is treated in §44.1. So the
4273   operator’s reach is precisely the local–global regime: below the boundary a signature is locally trivial
4274   at depth 𝑑 and the constructive synthesis of 𝔈 terminates; a stably essential signature is not killable
4275   by finite enlargement. Thus “not removable” does not mean “invisible,” and no transcendental
4276   Griffiths ceiling is asserted here. Which side a given 𝛼 falls on is read from whether its depth-𝑑
4277   obstruction is locally trivial — decided by the signature, not left to chance.

4278   The control-system reading. Equivalently 𝔈 is a closed-loop controller for representation mis-
4279   match: detect the residual mode, retune the participating clocks 𝜏𝑗 ↦→ 𝜏#𝑗 , enlarge the common
4280   cell where a rescaling cannot suffice (some obstructions need an added coordinate, or one tower
4281   level higher, not merely a rechart), re-run the fibers simultaneously 𝑋 # (𝜏) = 𝐹1# (𝜏), . . . , 𝐹𝑚
                                                                                                         # (𝜏) , and

4282   halt when exact focal closure certifies harmonization; the signature itself supplies the retuning law,
4283   closing the loop. One recharts until 𝛼 becomes an exact closing coordinate — not until the scalar
4284   symptom disappears.


4285   43    Formalization scope
4286   Formalization. The reflection for a general fiber is Lean-proved: FiniteWeightFiber formalizes the fi-
4287   nite duality-stable weight fiber and its carrier reflection (ledger fiber_det_one, per-place functional
4288   equation localPoly_reciprocal, axis fiber_reflection_axis, warp-invariance warpFiber), with
4289   Sym𝑟 (symFiber) and Rankin–Selberg (tensorFiber) as instances and the standard axiom footprint
4290   (App. B). So the functional-equation input of Proposition 57 is machine-checked at the general
4291   interface it actually consumes, not only for the Dirichlet model — and the completed-reflection
4292   assembly is machine-checked family-generally (FiniteWeightFiber.symTensorCompleted_FE,
4293   above), with the global strand-exchange input, step (2) of Prop. 74, machine-checked at the
4294   finite-stage bank (StrandExchange.bankProduct_exchange, completedBank_exchange) and the
4295   general dual-pair reciprocity at its exact interface (DualPairFiber). The E5 bridge is likewise
4296   machine-checked in the initial half-plane: CarrierTheta.theta_hasMellin_of_polynomial iden-
4297   tifies the full coefficient theta with its Dirichlet readout times the completion Mellin factor, while
4298   GlobalHelix.cpsPolynomialConductor_initialIdentification_pair simultaneously special-
4299   izes the primal and contragredient banks to the prescribed Gamma/conductor completion. The
4300   full nonempty Deligne-shift list, rather than only the one-shift specialization, is assembled for ev-
4301   ery CPS twist by GlobalHelix.cpsPolynomialAllTwists_fullCompletion3D_unified; its single
4302   conclusion also contains radial 3D reflection, both completed identifications, analytic continuation,
4303   strip bounds, and the functional equation for the strong pair built from the same 𝑊. Thus the
4304   analytic identification used by Prop. 55 is wired into the CPS completion surface rather than left

                                                             116
4305   as an unnamed manuscript transition. The remaining formalization scope is the final all-place
4306   arithmetic instantiation of the abstract Satake family, including the ramified local dictionaries;
4307   Prop. 55 proves that dictionary in the manuscript. The numerical experiments retained serve only
4308   as calibration and independent reproduction of the already-proved classical-𝐿 identification and its
4309   exact archimedean normalization (the archimedean two-clock and Poisson completion tied to the
4310   exact global 𝐿-values), governed by the exact gauge; the carrier/fiber rescaling reduces the residue
4311   reading to cell arithmetic.


4312   44    Hodge Connection
4313   The loss-ledger ↔ cycle-filtration correspondence signature-based cycle detection of §40 is preliminary;
4314   calibrating it (hodge_layer_calib.py) surfaced a structural question out of scope here. The
4315   carrier’s descent 3D → 2D → 1D books a loss ledger — height (ordinate), radius, angle — and its
4316   leading central jet factors, by BSD/Gross–Zagier [23, 24], into three invariants the census resolves
4317   independently: the order 𝑟 (vanishing multiplicity), the regulator Reg (the height/Abel–Jacobi datum),
4318   and |Sha| (the local–global obstruction). So each of three cycle-filtration layers ordinarily invisible
4319   to Hodge projection carries a distinct retained coordinate — a genuinely different phenomenon from
4320   the Hodge-visible detection, and the reason those results are marked preliminary. The organising
4321   principle is that no layer should remain invisible. This is theorem-level for semisimple carrier states,
4322   where the moment tower is jointly faithful (§44.1), and is the target for extension classes. Beyond |Sha|,
4323   the transcendental Ceresa/Gross–Schoen class — the modified diagonal in CH2 (𝐶 3 )0 , homologically
4324   trivial — is the tensor-cube test case for the derivative/height tower, where its Beilinson–Bloch
4325   height is related, in the relevant theorem-anchored triple-product settings, to a central 𝐿-derivative
4326   of 𝐻 1 (𝐶)⊗3 (Zhang [26]; Yuan–Zhang–Zhang [27]); the classical hyperelliptic control vanishes,
4327   while known nontrivial Ceresa/Gross–Schoen examples provide positive level-three controls. Its
4328   exact carrier landing and extension-tower faithfulness are developed in the companion paper [30]:
4329   the typed Lean capstone consumes the standard height identity and exact carrier identification
4330   and proves nonzero height, nonzero realized state, first visibility at depth three, and an explicit
4331   algebraic source. Initial results appear to affirm the arithmetic instance (hodge_griffiths_probe.py,
4332   App. B): the regulator/value channel fires for every homologically-trivial cycle in the census (no
4333   silent cycle), and the recursive tower already shows cycles absent at level one appearing at level
4334   ≥ 2. The companion paper [30] carries out the formal correspondence: arbitrary finite extension
4335   stacks are retained, the radial–Torelli–cycle bridge constructs higher-grade certified sources with
4336   exact realization, and the grade split assembles source exhaustion on the finite-extension dial.
4337   At depth three, CeresaGrossSchoenLanding.complete_landing proves the full implication from
4338   the standard height certificate to the carrier and cycle source. The Klein-quartic computation’s
4339   measured 𝐿-side is on record — forced sign −1 and central derivative 0.8299 ≠ 0, matching the
4340   known non-torsion of the cycle — while the decimal is not presented as a Lean theorem. The first
4341   unnamed rung, grade four, is mapped and crossed on the carrier. A further probe against a deeper
4342   cycle-filtration example produced the expected delayed tower signature 0, . . . , 0, ≠ 0: a class silent at
4343   depth 1 first fires at depth 2, recomputed from point-counting, its first nonzero slot matching the
4344   expected tower level of the class (tower_exhaustion_test.py, App. B). Define the carrier filtration
4345   by vanishing of the tower readouts 𝑇𝑗 ,

4356   identification below attach to a non-circular, machine-fixed object, not that the correspondence
4357   is itself deep. Moreover 𝐹car is the unique filtration whose graded pieces are cut out by the tower

4359   universal properties on the source class, it coincides with 𝐹car (blochBeilinson_coincides) —
4360   a conditional corollary that assumes no general existence of the (conjectural) Bloch–Beilinson
4361   filtration, which is stronger and cleaner than positing that existence. The structural retention
4362   input is now carried not only on semisimple values but on every finite normalized extension stack:
4363   GeneralExtensionRetention stores layers 𝑐ℓ ,𝑖 , pairs a layer ℓ with a moment depth 𝑑, and proves by
       Vandermonde separation that 𝑇⟨ℓ ,𝑑⟩ = 𝑖 𝑐ℓ ,𝑖 𝜆 𝑑𝑖 is jointly faithful (generalExtensionTower_exhaustive,
                                              Í

4365   generalExtension_retention). This theorem does not silently identify an arithmetic cycle with
4366   such a stack; that identification is the typed realization map required at each arithmetic landing.
4367   The remaining companion-paper input is therefore the analytic-to-cycle construction, beginning
4368   with the from-scratch triple-product central-derivative identity landing the Ceresa/Gross–Schoen
4369   height at level three (whose derivative-to-height step consumes Zhang [26] / Yuan–Zhang–
4370   Zhang [27]). Each arithmetic landing invoked is theorem-anchored — Tate and Gross–Zagier–
4371   Kolyvagin [24, 25] at depth one, the Gross–Schoen/Ceresa triple-product bridge at tensor depth
4372   three ([26, 27]). So the depth correspondence is a machine-checked theorem for the carrier filtra-
4373   tion 𝐹car and a conditional corollary for Bloch–Beilinson. The no-silent-layer input is precisely
       triviality of the carrier radical 𝑅 := 𝑑 ker 𝑇𝑑 (exhaustive_of_radical_trivial), which reduces
                                             Ñ
4374

4375   gradewise to a nondegeneracy obligation — a faithful regulator into an anisotropic height pairing
4376   (grade_visible_of_nondegenerate), discharged by Néron–Tate positivity at depth one.

4377   44.1   Cycle-filtration faithfulness: finite extension retention and the Ceresa frontier
4378   The structural half is unconditional. On the semisimple carrier state — the finite duality-stable weight
4379   fiber, an amplitude state 𝑐 over distinct clock frequencies {𝜆 𝑖 } — the symmetric-power/moment
       tower 𝑇𝑑 (𝑐) = 𝑖 𝑐 𝑖 𝜆 𝑖𝑑 is a jointly faithful coordinate system: distinct frequencies make the
                        Í
4380

       moment matrix Vandermonde, so 𝑑 ker 𝑇𝑑 = 0 and every nonzero state fires at some fi-
                                                    Ñ
4381

4382   nite level (CarrierTowerSeparation.momentTower_exhaustive, from momentTower_detects →
4383   momentTower_radical_trivial → exhaustive_of_radical_trivial; Lean). The same separa-
4384   tion now holds for arbitrary finite extension order. For a typed distinct clock bank, GeneralExtensionData
       stores a complete finite jet stack 𝑐ℓ ,𝑖 ; the tower decodes its natural index as (ℓ , 𝑑) and reads 𝑖 𝑐ℓ ,𝑖 𝜆 𝑑𝑖 .
                                                                                                          Í
4385

4386   Silence at every paired index therefore kills each layer separately, proving trivial radical, Exhaustive,
4387   and Retention (generalExtensionTower_detects, generalExtensionTower_exhaustive, generalExtension_re
4388   Lean). Thus the finite structural route covers semisimple values and all finite normalized jet layers
4389   with no Bloch–Beilinson input. For a homologically-trivial cycle the remaining obligation is precise:
4390   construct its typed finite extension datum and prove that the arithmetic derivative/height readouts


                                                       118
4391   agree with this paired tower. Retention then follows by transport rather than by a new no-silent-layer
4392   assumption.
4393       We do not place the transcendental (Abel–Jacobi-trivial) Griffiths class in 𝑅: that would require
4394   every 𝑇𝑑 to factor through the conventional Abel–Jacobi realization (radical_of_factorsThrough).
4395   Since the global Gross–Schoen height carries non-archimedean arithmetic data
4396   (Zhang’s admissible/metrized-graph local terms [26]) absent from that single-archimedean realiza-
4397   tion, factorization through 𝐴𝐽C cannot be assumed, and ruling it out is itself a separate non-factorization
4398   theorem, not established here. Absent one, homological- and Abel–Jacobi-triviality is an adversarial
4399   no-silent-layer benchmark (not_mem_radical_of_detectedPast), not a proven ceiling. One rung of
4400   this is unconditional: for the Fermat quartic the Ceresa class [𝐶] − [𝐶 − ] is homologically trivial yet is
4401   detected by a nonzero harmonic volume, Harris’s Abel–Jacobi-type invariant (Harris [29]; Ceresa [28]
4402   for the generic curve), so ker(cl) ⊈ ker(𝐴𝐽C ) — a class closed in the homology readout fires at the next
4403   retained coordinate, no conjecture. This establishes exactly the first rung (past cl); it does not show
4404   the 𝐴𝐽C -kernel itself is penetrated by 𝑇3 . For that deeper rung the explicit evidence currently cuts
4405   the other way: in the explicit bielliptic Picard family with a closed-form height, the Beilinson–Bloch
4406   height of the Ceresa cycle is proportional to the Néron–Tate height of its Abel–Jacobi point, vanishing
4407   exactly when that point is torsion (Laga–Shnidman [31]) — the Beilinson–Bloch height is controlled
4408   by the associated Néron–Tate coordinate there, so it does not penetrate ker 𝐴𝐽C . The genuine deeper
4409   target is therefore a class with 𝐴𝐽C (𝑧) zero or torsion yet a nonzero arithmetic level-three invariant —
4410   necessarily one where the non-archimedean local height dominates (Zhang’s metrized-graph terms)
4411   or where the finer ℓ -adic/Galois Ceresa class, not the archimedean height, is the retained coordinate.
4412   The companion’s typed Ceresa theorem now proves the exact analytic-to-cycle implication once
4413   this arithmetic certificate is supplied (CeresaGrossSchoenLanding.complete_landing) [30].
4414




                                                          119
4415       Appendix
4416   Conclusion
4417   What stands, and at what strength. The carrier system of Part I is proven and machine-checked
4418   end to end: projection with its ledger is a bĳection, sources are synthesized from finite data alone,
4419   vanishing is exact focal cancellation, and the transport is universal and functorial. The 𝑆(𝑡) term is
4420   proven to be the registration gap between the scaled carrier and the unit chart — the chart-defect
4421   compensation mechanism, described and discharged. Symmetric-power functoriality holds at
4422   every rank with niceness discharged on the carrier, and Sato–Tate for Maass forms follows on
4423   the Galois-free route. Beyond Endoscopy’s uniformity problem is reduced to a single magnitude
4424   bound and its obstruction identified as the orbital transform’s own clock, with a repair that scales.
4425   The worked-example part retains two conditional GRH deductions and now states their minimal
4426   dependencies explicitly. The helix midpoint is a geometric output of unique area-law scale balance
4427   and no drift. A native 3D zero is a completed fibre focal cancellation at physical height 𝑍 > 0,
4428   exactly the analytic 𝐿-zero at 𝜎∗ + 𝑖 log 𝑍; its finite-bank detector is exactly equivalent to finite
4429   harmonic-pencil rank drop. Both Gram operators have 𝐺 ⊗ 𝐼3 spatial lifts that preserve and reflect
4430   rank drop. The scalar fibre 𝛾 idC is a valid local coordinate detector. Lean now also defines one
4431   fixed symmetric operator on the completed 3D event type, proves its explicit event eigenvectors,
4432   and packages the two resolvent versions: 3D-zero/eigenvector and 1D-zero/3D-zero/eigenvector.
4433   This event-space assembly does not by itself route an arbitrary analytic zero into the event subtype.
4434   Lean proves that the old 3D identity premise is GRH conjoined with midpoint-free native coverage;
4435   it also proves that the old 1D routing disjunction is automatic and that its pointwise chart-to-kernel
4436   premise alone implies the critical-line conclusion.
4437        The global 𝑆(𝑡) coordinate law remains an exact theorem: it carries the carrier-scale census to the
4438   unit-chart census and matches jumps, residues, and multiplicities. Completing the analytic-coverage
4439   route requires proving the resolvent/spectral capture for the event-independent ambient carrier
                   (3)
4440   operator 𝐴 𝑝,𝑟 , or instantiating the same interface with another fixed self-adjoint operator, as stated by
4441   grh_of_selfAdjoint_resolvent_capture. This separation preserves the proved carrier geometry
4442   and registration results while making the zero-set identification boundary explicit.
4443        The thesis, restated at the end as at the start: the unit-1 chart is the compression, not the object.
4444   Working in the scaled three-dimensional frame turned the 𝑆(𝑡) registration into a theorem, the
4445   convergence gate into a chart artifact, and a stalled trace-formula estimate into an exact gauge.
4446   The next arithmetic work is in the Hodge companion paper: instantiating the typed cycle-to-jet
4447   realization and source packages on the desired geometric classes. The kernel now contains finite-
4448   extension retention, higher-grade certified source construction, the Ceresa/Gross–Schoen landing
4449   implication, and their unrestricted source-exhaustion assembly (§44.1). Everything else that remains
4450   is bookkeeping at its own site: the Lean formalization scope is recorded where the theorems live
4451   (§37, Prop. 57). The theorems are checked and the artifacts are public.


4452   A    The exact gauge on the archimedean uniformity

4455   functional equation and the trace variable is Poisson-summed, one must bound, uniformly in

4524   transform of the form (11) (with 𝐶 ≍ 𝜉 𝑦/𝑙 𝑓 2 and 𝐷 the local scale), bounded by Lemma 83,
4525   or at the sharp order by the expansion of Theorem 84. Here 𝑁 indexes the truncation order of

4529   by Theorem 84 gives (𝑙 𝑓 2 / 𝑦)𝑁 on the profile branch and the 𝜉 𝑀 on the phase branch; and the
4530   𝑦 ≍ 𝑋√support with the 𝑦 𝑑𝑦 factors supplies the 𝑋 2 and the +3, so the profile branch collects to
4531   (𝑙 𝑓 2 / 𝑋)𝑁−𝑀+3 . We carry this power-counting only to the point where each inner bound reduces,
4532   term by term, to the single magnitude estimate of Lemma 83 — the exact-gauge substitute for
4533   Altuğ’s oscillation estimate, which is the sole change from his Proposition 5.2 — whose constants
4534   𝐵𝜏,𝑚,𝑎 (Φ) and ∥𝐺 (𝑖) ∥ ∞ are finite and independent of (𝜉, 𝜈, 𝑙, 𝑓 , 𝑋); the full exponent bookkeeping is
4535   his.                                                                                                    □
4536       Every uniform constant in §A is one application of Lemma 83; the content of Altuğ’s Appendix A,
4537   from the exact-gauge standpoint, is that single magnitude estimate. Where Altuğ’s route controls the
4538   transform through the asymptotic expansion together with an oscillation bound on the remainder,
4539   the exact gauge replaces that oscillation bound by the triangle inequality in the coordinate that
4540   makes the integrand real: the whole (𝜉, 𝜈, 𝑙, 𝑓 , 𝑋)-uniformity then rests on the 𝑥-independence of
4541   the single line integral 𝐵𝜏,𝑚,𝑎 (Φ), with no cancellation estimate at any step.

4544   quoted in the text are reproduced below with the script that computes each.
4545   • Lemma 83 (the gauge bound), be_uniformity_certify.py. For a Gaussian Φ, 𝐵1,0,1 (Φ) = 0.686,
4546     and the certificate margin 𝑀(𝑥) = |𝐴(𝑥)| 𝑥 𝜏/2 /𝐵 satisfies sup𝑥 𝑀(𝑥) = 0.914 ≤ 1, uniformly across
4547     𝑥 = 𝐶 2 𝐷 ∈ [0.05, 2500] and (𝜏, 𝑚) ∈ {0.5, 1, 2, 4} × {0, 2}. The line integrand decays as 𝑒 −𝜋|𝑣|
4548     (𝑣 → +∞) and 𝑒 −𝜋|𝑣|/2 (𝑣 → −∞), so 𝐵𝜏,𝑚,𝑎 (Φ) < ∞ for every 𝜏 > 0.
4549   • Proposition 86 (the uniform constant), be_prop52_certify.py. The constant 𝐿 𝑀 = ∥𝜕𝑦𝑀 (𝐺(𝑦/𝑋) 𝑦 Ψ)∥ 𝐿1
4550     fits a uniform monomial 𝐿 𝑀 ∼ 𝐶 𝑀 (𝑙 𝑓 2 )𝑎 𝑀 (1 + 𝜉)𝑏 𝑀 𝑋 𝑔 𝑀 with 𝑎 𝑀 = 0.41, 0.05, −0.05 for 𝑀 = 1, 2, 3
4551     and 𝑏 𝑀 ≤ 0. The 𝑙 𝑓 2 -exponent 𝑎 𝑀 grows more slowly than 𝑀 (𝑑𝑎/𝑑𝑀 ≈ −0.23), so each
4552     integration by parts nets 𝜈−1 and the bound is summable — the standard-representation side
4553     of the productivity boundary. (This is the crude magnitude route; the sharp exponents of
4554     Proposition 86 follow from Theorem 84.)
4555   • The registration instruments (§9.10), st_mu6_gram.py, st_cf_lags.py, st_cell_phase.py.
4556     Four pre-registered tests of positional coupling between the zero events and the lattice layers,
4557     all null, as the proven ergodicity predicts. (1) Gram parity: violation rates 0.0728 vs 0.0720 at
4558     𝑁=5000 ticks — flat. (2) mod-6 alignment of the Gram defect: the run-1 signal (𝑝 = 0.0355,
4559     IID permutation, 𝑁=1200) fails to replicate under the autocorrelation-preserving circular-shift
4560     null at 𝑁=5000 (𝑝 = 0.058 full range, 𝑝 = 0.49 upper half); the IID null overstates significance
4561     for Rosser-block-correlated sequences — the circular shift is the correct null for alignment
4562     tests. (3) CF lags {7, 106, 113} (the 𝜋-convergent denominators): 66th percentile, 𝑝 = 0.32; the
4563     visible autocorrelation is short-range spacing rigidity. (4) Cell-phase kinks: the zeros’ phases
4564     𝑥 = frac(𝜃(𝛾)/𝜋) follow the smooth classical 𝑆-shape (mean 0.4980, the half-jump shift); density
4565     kinks at the carrier subdivision 𝑥 = 1/3, 2/3 are smaller than at control breakpoints (0.0396 vs
4566     0.0477). Method laws recorded: sampling at the chart’s own ticks aliases the carrier subdivision

4567     away (instruments must sample the carrier coordinate); and positional statistics test a claim the

4569   • The emergent clock (§30), mb_beat.py. The script scans the clock coordinate 𝜈clock = 2𝜈𝐽 , so
4570     its profile is 𝑒(−𝑦𝜈clock /4𝑙 𝑓 2 ) while the analytic 𝐽 of Prop. 86 uses 𝑒(−𝑦𝜈𝐽 /2𝑙 𝑓 2 ). The current
4571     estimator fits the continuous log-power profile log |𝑉(𝜈clock )| 2 with a degree-7 envelope plus
4572     the first two harmonics sharing one fundamental; the error audit compares one, two, and three
4573     harmonics. In that coordinate the fitted clock law is Δ𝜈clock = 0.524(𝑙 𝑓 2 )1.03 (𝑋/8)−1.04 (1 + 𝜉)0.00
4574     with 𝑅 2 = 1.000; equivalently Δ𝜈𝐽 = 12 Δ𝜈clock . Per-cell 𝜅 eff = 4𝑙 𝑓 2 /(𝑋Δ𝜈clock ) has mean 0.943,
4575     standard deviation 0.025, and range 0.895–0.971; the harmonic-truncation median period shift is
4576     2.4 × 10−4 (largest 6.7 × 10−3 on the weakest long-period cell). The legacy deep-dip estimator
4577     gave 0.533(𝑙 𝑓 2 )1.00 (𝑋/8)−0.98 (1 + 𝜉)0.02 at 𝑅 2 = 0.996. The rank sweep mb_beat.py ranks 13
4578     applies the same 𝑈𝑟 (𝑥) multiplier for 0 ≤ 𝑟 ≤ 13 and separates two masks: continuous clock
4579     cells and deep-event cells. On clock cells every rank has 𝑅 2 = 1.000, 𝑙 𝑓 2 -exponent 1.03–1.04, and
4580     𝑋-exponent −1.04–−1.03. The continuous clock is present in all 12 nonzero-𝜉 cells through 𝑟 = 9,
4581     then in 10, 9, 8, 8 cells for 𝑟 = 10, 11, 12, 13; deep productivity drops faster, from 10/12 at 𝑟 = 0 to
4582     3/9 and 3/8 at 𝑟 = 11, 12. Thus the high-rank degradation is event visibility, not a breakdown of
4583     the clock law. The Beyond-Endoscopy scaling test is therefore cell-wise: first certify the phase
4584     clock on each cell, then measure the productive deep-event yield inside the certified cells. The
4585     same run confirms that the deep-dip comb vanishes at 𝜉 = 0 for 𝑟 = 0 (the integrand is unimodal
4586     there).
4587   • The GL(3) clock lift, mb_gl3_clock_lift.py, mb_gl3_wall_lift.py, gl3_family.py. The
4588     GL(3) lift keeps the clock law but does not keep it as one scalar MB clock: the two trace
4589     coordinates carry separate clocks, and the diagonal readout combines them as 𝑄/(𝑆 𝑎 + 𝑆𝑏 ). The
4590     split-coordinate clock ratios are pinned at median 1.0000, 1.0000, 1.0000 for the 𝑎-, 𝑏-, and diagonal
4591     readouts, while the same-𝑏 scalar collapse gives 0.8983. The wall-lift scan shows a persistent
4592     clock but only partial scalar compression of the spread (base 𝑅2 = 0.541, full scalar-feature
4593     𝑅2 = 0.623–0.640 on this grid). The family scan pins all four tested GL(3) forms, with universal
4594     cells 1.0005𝜋 and across-form spread 0.0001𝜋. Thus the higher-rank scaling rule is vector-clock
4595     extraction plus productivity accounting, not a single GL(2)-style period.

4601     distinct spans is obstructed exactly by span inequality. For GL(2), the clock law is certified
4602     at 𝑅 2 ≥ 0.999 for 14/14 ranks while productive deep-cell yield ranges from 0.33 to 0.83. For

4604     anisotropic same-clock control has median 0.7966 on the 𝑏-axis. For GL(4), the vector clock
4605     passes 36/36 cells on each of the 𝑎, 𝑏, 𝑐 trace coordinates and 36/36 diagonal cells; the scalar
4606     controls have medians 0.9715 and 0.9319 on anisotropic 𝑏- and 𝑐-windows, confirming the formal
4607     scalar-collapse obstruction and preserving the vector readout as the scaling law. The productivity
